	import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import { useLayerStore, type LayerEntry } from '$lib/stores/layerStore';
	import { crosshairSlice } from '$lib/stores/crosshairSlice';
	import { ViewType, getViewTypeName } from '$lib/types/ViewType';
	import type { VolumeLayerGpuInfo, LayerSpec } from '$lib/api';

	// Props
	let { 
		layerId,
		viewType,
		onViewportChange
	}: { 
		layerId: string | null;
		viewType: ViewType;
		onViewportChange?: (viewType: ViewType, viewport: { scale: number; offset: [number, number] }) => void;
	} = $props();

	// State
	let canvasElement = $state<HTMLCanvasElement>();
	let viewScale = $state(1.0);
	let viewOffset = $state([0, 0] as [number, number]);
	let isDragging = $state(false);
	let lastPointerPos = $state<[number, number] | null>(null);
	let containerSize = $state({ width: 512, height: 512 });
	let isRenderLoopRunning = $state(false);
	let animationFrameId: number | null = null;
	let gpuInitialized = $state(false);
	let renderTargetCreated = $state(false);
	
	// Track view center separately from crosshair
	let viewCenter = $state<[number, number, number] | null>(null);
	
	// Slice position state
	let slicePosition = $state(0); // Current slice position in mm
	let sliceMin = $state(-100); // Min slice position
	let sliceMax = $state(100); // Max slice position
	let sliceStep = $state(1); // Step size in mm

	// Helper to get layer ID from spec
	function getLayerIdFromSpec(spec: LayerSpec): string | null {
		if (spec && 'Volume' in spec) {
			return spec.Volume.id;
		}
		return null;
	}
	
	// Store state - make it reactive
	let layerStoreState = $state(useLayerStore.getState());
	
	// Get layer from store using a derived value for robust reactivity
	let layerEntry = $derived(
		layerId ? layerStoreState.layers.find((l: LayerEntry) => getLayerIdFromSpec(l.spec) === layerId) || null : null
	);
	

	// Get current crosshair position - make it reactive
	let crosshairState = $state(crosshairSlice.getState());
	// Default to null if no crosshair set (will be updated when volume loads)
	let crosshairPos = $derived(crosshairState.crosshairWorldCoord);

	// Canvas resize observer
	let resizeObserver: ResizeObserver | null = null;

	// Initialize GPU rendering
	async function initializeGPU() {
		try {
			if (!gpuInitialized) {
				console.log('Initializing GPU render loop...');
				await coreApi.init_render_loop();
				gpuInitialized = true;
			}
			
			// Create render target for this view
			// DISABLED: The main layout already creates a 512x512 render target
			// TODO: Support multiple render targets or dynamic sizing
			if (!renderTargetCreated && containerSize.width > 0 && containerSize.height > 0) {
				// The main layout creates a 512x512 render target
				// TODO: Support multiple render targets or dynamic sizing
				renderTargetCreated = true;
			}
		} catch (err) {
			console.error('Failed to initialize GPU:', err);
		}
	}

	// Setup view-specific parameters
	async function setupViewParameters() {
		if (!layerEntry?.gpu) return;
		
		// Wait for crosshair to be initialized
		if (!crosshairPos) {
			console.log('[OrthogonalViewGPU] Crosshair not yet initialized, skipping setup');
			return;
		}
		
		// Initialize view center if not set
		if (!viewCenter) {
			viewCenter = [...crosshairPos];
			console.log('[OrthogonalViewGPU] Initialized view center to:', viewCenter);
		}

		const { width, height } = containerSize;
		const aspectRatio = width / height;
		
		// Create orthographic projection matrix based on view scale and offset
		const scale = viewScale * 2;
		const viewProj = [
			scale / width, 0, 0, 0,
			0, scale / height, 0, 0,
			0, 0, 1, 0,
			-viewOffset[0] * scale / width, -viewOffset[1] * scale / height, 0, 1
		];

		// Get volume dimensions from layer info
		const volumeDim = layerEntry.gpu.dim;
		
		// DEBUG: Log the actual GPU metadata
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Volume metadata from GPU:`, {
			dim: [...layerEntry.gpu.dim],  // Spread to unwrap proxy
			spacing: [...layerEntry.gpu.spacing],  // Spread to unwrap proxy
			origin: [...layerEntry.gpu.origin]  // Spread to unwrap proxy
		});
		
		// Calculate view plane normal and distance based on view type
		let viewPlaneNormal: number[];
		let viewPlaneDistance: number;
		let viewPlaneIndex: number;
		
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				viewPlaneNormal = [0, 0, 1, 0];
				viewPlaneDistance = crosshairPos[2];
				viewPlaneIndex = 2;
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				viewPlaneNormal = [0, 1, 0, 0];
				viewPlaneDistance = crosshairPos[1];
				viewPlaneIndex = 1;
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				viewPlaneNormal = [1, 0, 0, 0];
				viewPlaneDistance = crosshairPos[0];
				viewPlaneIndex = 0;
				break;
		}

		// Update frame for synchronized view
		// Map ViewType to plane_id (0=Axial, 1=Coronal, 2=Sagittal)
		const planeId = viewType as 0 | 1 | 2;
		
		// Calculate view dimensions in mm based on actual volume dimensions
		// Get volume bounds from GPU info
		const volumeDims = layerEntry.gpu.dim;
		const volumeSpacing = layerEntry.gpu.spacing;
		const volumeOrigin = layerEntry.gpu.origin;
		
		// Calculate volume bounds in world space (mm)
		// The spacing can be positive or negative to indicate direction
		const volumeBounds = {
			x: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[0], volumeOrigin[0] + (volumeDims[0] - 1) * volumeSpacing[0]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[0], volumeOrigin[0] + (volumeDims[0] - 1) * volumeSpacing[0]) },
			y: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[1], volumeOrigin[1] + (volumeDims[1] - 1) * volumeSpacing[1]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[1], volumeOrigin[1] + (volumeDims[1] - 1) * volumeSpacing[1]) },
			z: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[2], volumeOrigin[2] + (volumeDims[2] - 1) * volumeSpacing[2]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[2], volumeOrigin[2] + (volumeDims[2] - 1) * volumeSpacing[2]) }
		};
		
		// DEBUG: Log the calculated bounds
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Calculated volume bounds:`, {
			x: `[${volumeBounds.x.min.toFixed(3)}, ${volumeBounds.x.max.toFixed(3)}]`,
			y: `[${volumeBounds.y.min.toFixed(3)}, ${volumeBounds.y.max.toFixed(3)}]`,
			z: `[${volumeBounds.z.min.toFixed(3)}, ${volumeBounds.z.max.toFixed(3)}]`
		});
		
		// Calculate the natural dimensions for each view type
		let naturalWidthMm: number;
		let naturalHeightMm: number;
		
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// XY plane
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.x.max - volumeBounds.x.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.y.max - volumeBounds.y.min;
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// XZ plane
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.x.max - volumeBounds.x.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.z.max - volumeBounds.z.min;
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// YZ plane
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.y.max - volumeBounds.y.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.z.max - volumeBounds.z.min;
				break;
		}
		
		// DEBUG: Log natural dimensions before padding
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Natural dimensions before padding: ${naturalWidthMm.toFixed(3)} x ${naturalHeightMm.toFixed(3)} mm`);
		
		// Add some padding (10% on each side)
		const padding = 1.2;
		naturalWidthMm *= padding;
		naturalHeightMm *= padding;
		
		// DEBUG: Log after padding
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] After padding (${padding}x): ${naturalWidthMm.toFixed(3)} x ${naturalHeightMm.toFixed(3)} mm`);
		
		// Apply view scale (zoom)
		const viewWidthMm = naturalWidthMm / viewScale;
		const viewHeightMm = naturalHeightMm / viewScale;
		
		// DEBUG: Log final view dimensions
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Final view dimensions (scale=${viewScale}): ${viewWidthMm.toFixed(3)} x ${viewHeightMm.toFixed(3)} mm`);
		
		// Update slice bounds based on view type
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// Z axis (Inferior to Superior)
				sliceMin = volumeBounds.z.min;
				sliceMax = volumeBounds.z.max;
				slicePosition = crosshairPos[2];
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// Y axis (Posterior to Anterior)
				sliceMin = volumeBounds.y.min;
				sliceMax = volumeBounds.y.max;
				slicePosition = crosshairPos[1];
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// X axis (Right to Left)
				sliceMin = volumeBounds.x.min;
				sliceMax = volumeBounds.x.max;
				slicePosition = crosshairPos[0];
				break;
		}
		
		// Log current crosshair position for debugging
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Setting up view for ${getViewTypeName(viewType)}`);
		console.log(`  Crosshair position: [${crosshairPos[0]}, ${crosshairPos[1]}, ${crosshairPos[2]}]`);
		console.log(`  View dimensions: ${viewWidthMm.toFixed(1)} x ${viewHeightMm.toFixed(1)} mm`);
		console.log(`  Volume bounds:`, volumeBounds);
		
		// TEMPORARY FIX: Force crosshair to volume center if it's outside bounds
		const volumeCenterX = (volumeBounds.x.min + volumeBounds.x.max) / 2;
		const volumeCenterY = (volumeBounds.y.min + volumeBounds.y.max) / 2;
		const volumeCenterZ = (volumeBounds.z.min + volumeBounds.z.max) / 2;
		
		if (crosshairPos[0] < volumeBounds.x.min || crosshairPos[0] > volumeBounds.x.max ||
		    crosshairPos[1] < volumeBounds.y.min || crosshairPos[1] > volumeBounds.y.max ||
		    crosshairPos[2] < volumeBounds.z.min || crosshairPos[2] > volumeBounds.z.max) {
			console.warn(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Crosshair outside volume bounds! Resetting to center: [${volumeCenterX}, ${volumeCenterY}, ${volumeCenterZ}]`);
			crosshairSlice.getState().setCrosshairWorldCoord([volumeCenterX, volumeCenterY, volumeCenterZ]);
			return; // Skip this frame, will re-render with correct crosshair
		}
		
		// Set view plane first
		await coreApi.set_view_plane(planeId);
		
		// Set crosshair position for the shader
		// Use the actual slice position, not the original crosshair position
		let shaderCrosshair: [number, number, number];
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// Update Z to slice position
				shaderCrosshair = [crosshairPos[0], crosshairPos[1], slicePosition];
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// Update Y to slice position
				shaderCrosshair = [crosshairPos[0], slicePosition, crosshairPos[2]];
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// Update X to slice position
				shaderCrosshair = [slicePosition, crosshairPos[1], crosshairPos[2]];
				break;
		}
		await coreApi.set_crosshair(shaderCrosshair);
		
		
		// For now, pass the natural dimensions without adjustment
		// TODO: The aspect ratio preservation should be handled in the renderer
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] View dimensions:`, {
			width: viewWidthMm.toFixed(3),
			height: viewHeightMm.toFixed(3),
			aspect: (viewWidthMm / viewHeightMm).toFixed(3),
			viewport: { width: containerSize.width, height: containerSize.height, aspect: (containerSize.width / containerSize.height).toFixed(3) }
		});
		
		// Use view center for in-plane coordinates, slicePosition for slice coordinate
		let frameCenter: [number, number, number];
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// Keep X,Y from view center, use slicePosition for Z
				frameCenter = [viewCenter[0], viewCenter[1], slicePosition];
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// Keep X,Z from view center, use slicePosition for Y
				frameCenter = [viewCenter[0], slicePosition, viewCenter[2]];
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// Keep Y,Z from view center, use slicePosition for X
				frameCenter = [slicePosition, viewCenter[1], viewCenter[2]];
				break;
		}
		
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Frame center for ${getViewTypeName(viewType)}:`, frameCenter);
		console.log(`  View center: [${viewCenter[0].toFixed(1)}, ${viewCenter[1].toFixed(1)}, ${viewCenter[2].toFixed(1)}]`);
		console.log(`  Slice position: ${slicePosition.toFixed(1)}`);
		console.log(`  Crosshair shader: [${shaderCrosshair[0].toFixed(1)}, ${shaderCrosshair[1].toFixed(1)}, ${shaderCrosshair[2].toFixed(1)}]`);
		
		await coreApi.update_frame_for_synchronized_view(
			viewWidthMm,
			viewHeightMm,
			frameCenter,
			planeId
		);
	}

	// Track if layer is already added
	let layerAdded = false;
	
	// Add layer to render state
	async function addLayerToRenderState() {
		if (!layerEntry?.gpu || !renderTargetCreated || layerAdded) return;
		

		try {
			// Add render layer with correct parameters
			const textureCoords = [
				layerEntry.gpu.texture_coords.u_min,
				layerEntry.gpu.texture_coords.v_min,
				layerEntry.gpu.texture_coords.u_max,
				layerEntry.gpu.texture_coords.v_max
			];
			
			await coreApi.add_render_layer(
				layerEntry.gpu.atlas_layer_index,
				1.0, // opacity
				textureCoords
			);
			
			layerAdded = true;
		} catch (err) {
			console.error('Failed to add layer to render state:', err);
			// If we get a max layer error, it might mean the layer was already added
			if (err && typeof err === 'object' && 'Internal' in err) {
				const internal = err.Internal;
				if (internal && internal.details && internal.details.includes('Maximum layer count exceeded')) {
					console.warn('Layer might already be added, continuing...');
					layerAdded = true;
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Render frame
	async function renderFrame() {
		if (!canvasElement || !layerEntry?.gpu || !renderTargetCreated) return;
		
		// Ensure we have valid dimensions
		if (containerSize.width === 0 || containerSize.height === 0) {
			console.warn('Skipping render - container size is 0x0');
			return;
		}
		
		// Wait for crosshair to be initialized
		if (!crosshairPos) {
			console.log('[OrthogonalViewGPU] Skipping render - crosshair not initialized');
			return;
		}
		

		try {
			// Update view parameters
			await setupViewParameters();
			
			// Render to offscreen buffer and get image
			const imageDataUrl = await coreApi.render_to_image();
			
			// Parse the data URL
			if (imageDataUrl.startsWith('data:image/raw-rgba;base64,')) {
				const base64Data = imageDataUrl.substring('data:image/raw-rgba;base64,'.length);
				const binaryData = atob(base64Data);
				const bytes = new Uint8Array(binaryData.length);
				for (let i = 0; i < binaryData.length; i++) {
					bytes[i] = binaryData.charCodeAt(i);
				}

				// Get canvas context
				const ctx = canvasElement.getContext('2d');
				if (!ctx) return;

				// Validate buffer size
				// Note: The render loop might return a fixed size buffer (e.g., 352x256)
				// regardless of what we request
				const expectedSize = containerSize.width * containerSize.height * 4; // RGBA = 4 bytes per pixel
				const actualPixelCount = bytes.length / 4;
				
				if (bytes.length !== expectedSize) {
					console.warn(`Buffer size mismatch: got ${bytes.length} bytes, canvas: ${containerSize.width}x${containerSize.height} - will scale to fit`);
					
					// Calculate actual render dimensions from buffer size
					// Buffer size = width * height * 4 (RGBA)
					const pixelCount = bytes.length / 4;
					
					// Try common aspect ratios and sizes
					let renderWidth = 0;
					let renderHeight = 0;
					
					// Try some common dimensions
					const possibleSizes = [
						[512, 512], [256, 256], [352, 256], [256, 352],
						[512, 256], [256, 512], [512, 176], [176, 512],
						[352, 256] // Exact match for 360448 bytes
					];
					
					for (const [w, h] of possibleSizes) {
						if (w * h === pixelCount) {
							renderWidth = w;
							renderHeight = h;
							break;
						}
					}
					
					// If not found, try to find any valid dimensions
					if (renderWidth === 0) {
						// Try dividing by common widths
						for (const width of [512, 256, 352, 480, 640]) {
							if (pixelCount % width === 0) {
								const height = pixelCount / width;
								if (height === Math.floor(height)) {
									renderWidth = width;
									renderHeight = height;
									break;
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if (renderWidth > 0 && renderHeight > 0) {
						// Create ImageData with render target dimensions
						const imageData = new ImageData(
							new Uint8ClampedArray(bytes.buffer),
							renderWidth,
							renderHeight
						);
						
						// Check for content in the rendered image
						const pixels = new Uint8ClampedArray(bytes.buffer);
						let hasContent = false;
						let uniqueColors = new Set();
						let samplePixels = [];
						
						// Sample some pixels to check for variation
						for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(pixels.length, 10000); i += 4) {
							const color = `${pixels[i]},${pixels[i+1]},${pixels[i+2]}`;
							uniqueColors.add(color);
							if (samplePixels.length < 5) {
								samplePixels.push(`[${i/4}]: R=${pixels[i]} G=${pixels[i+1]} B=${pixels[i+2]} A=${pixels[i+3]}`);
							}
							if (pixels[i] > 0 || pixels[i+1] > 0 || pixels[i+2] > 0) {
								hasContent = true;
							}
						}
						
						// Scale to fit canvas
						const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
						tempCanvas.width = renderWidth;
						tempCanvas.height = renderHeight;
						const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');
						if (tempCtx) {
							tempCtx.putImageData(imageData, 0, 0);
							// Clear canvas first
							ctx.clearRect(0, 0, containerSize.width, containerSize.height);
							
							// Calculate aspect-preserving dimensions
							const sourceAspect = renderWidth / renderHeight;
							const targetAspect = containerSize.width / containerSize.height;
							
							let drawWidth = containerSize.width;
							let drawHeight = containerSize.height;
							let drawX = 0;
							let drawY = 0;
							
							if (sourceAspect > targetAspect) {
								// Source is wider - fit width, letterbox height
								drawHeight = containerSize.width / sourceAspect;
								drawY = (containerSize.height - drawHeight) / 2;
							} else if (sourceAspect < targetAspect) {
								// Source is taller - fit height, pillarbox width
								drawWidth = containerSize.height * sourceAspect;
								drawX = (containerSize.width - drawWidth) / 2;
							}
							
							// Draw scaled image with aspect ratio preserved
							ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas, 0, 0, renderWidth, renderHeight, drawX, drawY, drawWidth, drawHeight);
						}
					} else {
						console.warn('Could not determine buffer dimensions for size:', bytes.length, '- skipping render');
					}
				} else {
					// Create ImageData from raw RGBA
					const imageData = new ImageData(
						new Uint8ClampedArray(bytes.buffer),
						containerSize.width,
						containerSize.height
					);
					
					// Debug: Check if image has any non-zero pixels
					const pixels = new Uint8ClampedArray(bytes.buffer);
					let hasContent = false;
					for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(100, pixels.length); i += 4) {
						if (pixels[i] > 0 || pixels[i+1] > 0 || pixels[i+2] > 0) {
							hasContent = true;
							break;
						}
					}
					

					// Draw to canvas with aspect ratio preservation
					// Since render target is 512x512 (square), preserve aspect ratio
					const sourceAspect = 1.0; // 512x512 is square
					const targetAspect = containerSize.width / containerSize.height;
					
					let drawWidth = containerSize.width;
					let drawHeight = containerSize.height;
					let drawX = 0;
					let drawY = 0;
					
					if (sourceAspect > targetAspect) {
						// Source is wider - fit width, letterbox height
						drawHeight = containerSize.width / sourceAspect;
						drawY = (containerSize.height - drawHeight) / 2;
					} else if (sourceAspect < targetAspect) {
						// Source is taller - fit height, pillarbox width
						drawWidth = containerSize.height * sourceAspect;
						drawX = (containerSize.width - drawWidth) / 2;
					}
					
					// Create temp canvas to hold the image data
					const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
					tempCanvas.width = containerSize.width;
					tempCanvas.height = containerSize.height;
					const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');
					if (tempCtx) {
						tempCtx.putImageData(imageData, 0, 0);
						
						// Clear and draw with proper aspect ratio
						ctx.clearRect(0, 0, containerSize.width, containerSize.height);
						ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas, 0, 0, containerSize.width, containerSize.height, drawX, drawY, drawWidth, drawHeight);
					}
				}
			}
		} catch (err) {
			console.error('Render frame error:', err);
		}
	}

	// Start render loop
	function startRenderLoop() {
		if (isRenderLoopRunning) return;
		
		isRenderLoopRunning = true;
		
		// Render once immediately
		renderFrame().then(() => {
			// For now, don't use continuous animation - just render on changes
			// We'll add proper dirty tracking later
		});
	}

	// Stop render loop
	function stopRenderLoop() {
		isRenderLoopRunning = false;
		if (animationFrameId !== null) {
			cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId);
			animationFrameId = null;
		}
	}

	// Debounced resize handler
	const handleResizeDebounced = debounce(async (width: number, height: number) => {
		const newWidth = Math.max(256, Math.floor(width));
		const newHeight = Math.max(256, Math.floor(height));
		
		if (newWidth > 0 && newHeight > 0 && (newWidth !== containerSize.width || newHeight !== containerSize.height)) {
			containerSize = { width: newWidth, height: newHeight };
			
			// Update canvas size
			if (canvasElement) {
				canvasElement.width = newWidth;
				canvasElement.height = newHeight;
			}
			
			// Recreate render target with new size
			renderTargetCreated = false;
			await initializeGPU();
			
			// Re-render with new size
			if (isRenderLoopRunning && layerEntry?.gpu) {
				await renderFrame();
			}
		}
	}, 250);

	// Convert canvas coordinates to world coordinates
	function canvasToWorld(canvasX: number, canvasY: number): [number, number, number] | null {
		if (!layerEntry?.gpu || !crosshairPos) return null;
		
		// Get canvas dimensions
		const rect = canvasElement?.getBoundingClientRect();
		if (!rect) return null;
		
		// Convert to normalized device coordinates (-1 to 1)
		const ndcX = (canvasX / rect.width) * 2 - 1;
		const ndcY = -((canvasY / rect.height) * 2 - 1); // Flip Y
		
		// Get view parameters
		const volumeDims = layerEntry.gpu.dim;
		const volumeSpacing = layerEntry.gpu.spacing;
		const volumeOrigin = layerEntry.gpu.origin;
		
		// Calculate volume bounds
		const volumeBounds = {
			x: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[0], volumeOrigin[0] + (volumeDims[0] - 1) * volumeSpacing[0]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[0], volumeOrigin[0] + (volumeDims[0] - 1) * volumeSpacing[0]) },
			y: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[1], volumeOrigin[1] + (volumeDims[1] - 1) * volumeSpacing[1]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[1], volumeOrigin[1] + (volumeDims[1] - 1) * volumeSpacing[1]) },
			z: { min: Math.min(volumeOrigin[2], volumeOrigin[2] + (volumeDims[2] - 1) * volumeSpacing[2]),
			     max: Math.max(volumeOrigin[2], volumeOrigin[2] + (volumeDims[2] - 1) * volumeSpacing[2]) }
		};
		
		// Get natural dimensions for this view
		let naturalWidthMm: number;
		let naturalHeightMm: number;
		
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.x.max - volumeBounds.x.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.y.max - volumeBounds.y.min;
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.x.max - volumeBounds.x.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.z.max - volumeBounds.z.min;
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				naturalWidthMm = volumeBounds.y.max - volumeBounds.y.min;
				naturalHeightMm = volumeBounds.z.max - volumeBounds.z.min;
				break;
		}
		
		// Add padding
		const padding = 1.2;
		naturalWidthMm *= padding;
		naturalHeightMm *= padding;
		
		// Apply view scale
		const viewWidthMm = naturalWidthMm / viewScale;
		const viewHeightMm = naturalHeightMm / viewScale;
		
		// Convert NDC to world coordinates based on view type
		const halfWidth = viewWidthMm / 2;
		const halfHeight = viewHeightMm / 2;
		
		let worldX = crosshairPos[0];
		let worldY = crosshairPos[1];
		let worldZ = crosshairPos[2];
		
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// XY plane - mouse moves X and Y
				worldX = crosshairPos[0] + ndcX * halfWidth;
				worldY = crosshairPos[1] - ndcY * halfHeight; // Negative because Y is flipped
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// XZ plane - mouse moves X and Z
				worldX = crosshairPos[0] + ndcX * halfWidth;
				worldZ = crosshairPos[2] - ndcY * halfHeight; // Negative because Z is flipped
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// YZ plane - mouse moves Y and Z
				worldY = crosshairPos[1] + ndcX * halfWidth;
				worldZ = crosshairPos[2] - ndcY * halfHeight; // Negative because Z is flipped
				break;
		}
		
		return [worldX, worldY, worldZ];
	}

	// Mouse/pointer handlers
	function handlePointerDown(event: PointerEvent) {
		if (event.button === 0) { // Left click
			// Calculate mouse position relative to canvas
			const rect = canvasElement?.getBoundingClientRect();
			if (rect) {
				const canvasX = event.clientX - rect.left;
				const canvasY = event.clientY - rect.top;
				
				// Convert to world coordinates and update crosshair
				const worldCoords = canvasToWorld(canvasX, canvasY);
				if (worldCoords) {
					crosshairSlice.getState().setCrosshairWorldCoord(worldCoords);
				}
			}
			
			// Start dragging for pan - DISABLED for now
			// isDragging = true;
			// lastPointerPos = [event.clientX, event.clientY];
			// (event.target as HTMLElement).setPointerCapture(event.pointerId);
		}
	}

	function handlePointerMove(event: PointerEvent) {
		// Update mouse world coordinates for status bar
		const rect = canvasElement?.getBoundingClientRect();
		if (rect) {
			const canvasX = event.clientX - rect.left;
			const canvasY = event.clientY - rect.top;
			const worldCoords = canvasToWorld(canvasX, canvasY);
			
			// Dispatch custom event for StatusBar
			if (worldCoords) {
				window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('mouseworldcoord', { 
					detail: worldCoords 
				}));
			}
		}
		
		// Handle dragging for pan - DISABLED for now
		// if (isDragging && lastPointerPos) {
		// 	const dx = event.clientX - lastPointerPos[0];
		// 	const dy = event.clientY - lastPointerPos[1];
		// 	
		// 	viewOffset = [
		// 		viewOffset[0] + dx / viewScale,
		// 		viewOffset[1] + dy / viewScale
		// 	];
		// 	
		// 	lastPointerPos = [event.clientX, event.clientY];
		// 	
		// 	onViewportChange?.(viewType, { scale: viewScale, offset: viewOffset });
		// }
	}

	function handlePointerUp(event: PointerEvent) {
		isDragging = false;
		lastPointerPos = null;
		(event.target as HTMLElement).releasePointerCapture(event.pointerId);
	}
	
	function handlePointerLeave(event: PointerEvent) {
		// Clear mouse coordinates when leaving canvas
		window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('mouseworldcoord', { 
			detail: null 
		}));
	}

	function handleWheel(event: WheelEvent) {
		event.preventDefault();
		const scaleFactor = event.deltaY > 0 ? 0.9 : 1.1;
		viewScale = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(10, viewScale * scaleFactor));
		
		onViewportChange?.(viewType, { scale: viewScale, offset: viewOffset });
	}
	
	// Handle slider change
	function handleSliderChange(event: Event) {
		const target = event.target as HTMLInputElement;
		const newPosition = parseFloat(target.value);
		
		// Skip if crosshair not initialized
		if (!crosshairPos) return;
		
		// Debug logging
		console.log(`[OrthogonalViewGPU] Slider change for ${getViewTypeName(viewType)}`);
		console.log(`  Old crosshair: [${crosshairPos[0].toFixed(1)}, ${crosshairPos[1].toFixed(1)}, ${crosshairPos[2].toFixed(1)}]`);
		console.log(`  New slider position: ${newPosition.toFixed(1)}`);
		
		// Update crosshair position based on view type
		let newCrosshair: [number, number, number] = [...crosshairPos];
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				newCrosshair[2] = newPosition;
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				newCrosshair[1] = newPosition;
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				newCrosshair[0] = newPosition;
				break;
		}
		
		console.log(`  New crosshair: [${newCrosshair[0].toFixed(1)}, ${newCrosshair[1].toFixed(1)}, ${newCrosshair[2].toFixed(1)}]`);
		
		// For now, don't update global crosshair - just update local slice position
		// This prevents other views from jumping when we move the slider
		// crosshairSlice.getState().setCrosshairWorldCoord(newCrosshair);
		
		// Update local slice position immediately for responsive UI
		slicePosition = newPosition;
		
		// Trigger a re-render with the new slice position
		if (isRenderLoopRunning && layerEntry?.gpu) {
			setupViewParameters().then(() => {
				renderFrame();
			});
		}
	}

	// React to layer changes
	$effect(() => {
		if (layerEntry?.gpu && gpuInitialized && renderTargetCreated && containerSize.width > 0 && containerSize.height > 0) {
			// Reset layer added flag if layer changed
			const currentLayerId = getLayerIdFromSpec(layerEntry.spec);
			if (currentLayerId !== layerId) {
				layerAdded = false;
			}
			
			addLayerToRenderState().then(() => {
				startRenderLoop();
			});
		} else {
			stopRenderLoop();
		}
	});

	// React to crosshair changes
	$effect(() => {
		// Update view parameters and re-render when crosshair changes
		if (isRenderLoopRunning && layerEntry?.gpu && crosshairPos) {
			console.log('[OrthogonalViewGPU] Crosshair changed, updating view parameters');
			setupViewParameters().then(() => {
				renderFrame();
			});
		}
	});

	// Lifecycle
	onMount(async () => {
		// Subscribe to store changes
		const unsubscribeLayerStore = useLayerStore.subscribe((state) => {
			layerStoreState = state;
		});
		
		// Subscribe to crosshair changes
		const unsubscribeCrosshair = crosshairSlice.subscribe((state) => {
			crosshairState = state;
		});
		
		if (canvasElement) {
			// Wait a frame to ensure the layout is complete
			await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
			
			// Try getting dimensions from parent container first
			const parent = canvasElement.parentElement;
			const parentRect = parent?.getBoundingClientRect();
			
			// Set initial canvas size
			const rect = canvasElement.getBoundingClientRect();
			const width = Math.max(256, Math.floor(parentRect?.width || rect.width || 256));
			const height = Math.max(256, Math.floor(parentRect?.height || rect.height || 256));
			
			canvasElement.width = width;
			canvasElement.height = height;
			containerSize = { width, height };
			
			// Initialize GPU after we have dimensions
			await initializeGPU();
			
			// Setup resize observer
			resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver((entries) => {
				const entry = entries[0];
				const { width, height } = entry.contentRect;
				handleResizeDebounced(Math.floor(width), Math.floor(height));
			});
			resizeObserver.observe(canvasElement.parentElement || canvasElement);
		}
		
		return () => {
			stopRenderLoop();
			resizeObserver?.disconnect();
			handleResizeDebounced.cancel();
			unsubscribeLayerStore();
			unsubscribeCrosshair();
			
			// Clean up GPU resources
			if (layerId && layerEntry?.gpu) {
				// TODO: Add API call to remove render layer when available
				// coreApi.remove_render_layer(layerId).catch(console.error);
			}
		};
	});
</script>

<div class="orthogonal-view" data-view-type={viewType}>
	<!-- View label -->
	<div class="view-label">{getViewTypeName(viewType)}</div>
	
	<!-- Error/loading overlays -->
	{#if !layerEntry}
		<div class="overlay loading">No layer selected</div>
	{:else if layerEntry.error}
		<div class="overlay error">Error: {layerEntry.error instanceof Error ? layerEntry.error.message : 'Unknown error'}</div>
	{:else if layerEntry.isLoadingGpu}
		<div class="overlay loading">Loading GPU resources...</div>
	{:else if !layerEntry.gpu}
		<div class="overlay loading">Waiting for GPU resources...</div>
	{:else if !gpuInitialized}
		<div class="overlay loading">Initializing GPU...</div>
	{:else}
		{#if !renderTargetCreated}
			<div class="overlay loading">Creating render target...</div>
		{/if}
	{/if}

	<!-- Canvas -->
	<canvas
		bind:this={canvasElement}
		class="view-canvas"
		onpointerdown={handlePointerDown}
		onpointermove={handlePointerMove}
		onpointerup={handlePointerUp}
		onpointerleave={handlePointerLeave}
		onpointercancel={handlePointerUp}
		onwheel={handleWheel}
		data-testid={`canvas-${getViewTypeName(viewType).toLowerCase()}`}
	></canvas>

	<!-- Orientation indicators -->
	<div class="orientation-markers">
		{#if viewType === ViewType.Axial}
			<span class="marker top">A</span>
			<span class="marker bottom">P</span>
			<span class="marker left">R</span>
			<span class="marker right">L</span>
		{:else if viewType === ViewType.Coronal}
			<span class="marker top">S</span>
			<span class="marker bottom">I</span>
			<span class="marker left">R</span>
			<span class="marker right">L</span>
		{:else if viewType === ViewType.Sagittal}
			<span class="marker top">S</span>
			<span class="marker bottom">I</span>
			<span class="marker left">P</span>
			<span class="marker right">A</span>
		{/if}
	</div>
	
	<!-- Slice slider -->
	{#if layerEntry?.gpu}
		<div class="slice-slider-container">
			<div class="slice-info">
				<span class="slice-label">
					{#if viewType === ViewType.Axial}
						I/S:
					{:else if viewType === ViewType.Coronal}
						P/A:
					{:else}
						R/L:
					{/if}
				</span>
				<span class="slice-value">{slicePosition.toFixed(1)} mm</span>
			</div>
			<input
				type="range"
				class="slice-slider"
				min={sliceMin}
				max={sliceMax}
				step={sliceStep}
				value={slicePosition}
				oninput={handleSliderChange}
			/>
		</div>
	{/if}
</div>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/views/VolumeView.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	/**
	 * @component VolumeView
	 * @description Three-panel orthogonal view for neuroimaging volumes
	 * 
	 * Displays Axial, Coronal, and Sagittal views in a synchronized layout
	 * with shared crosshair and layer state.
	 */
	import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
	import type { ComponentContainer } from 'golden-layout';
	import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import { useLayerStore } from '$lib/stores/layerStore';
	import { useVolumeStore } from '$lib/stores/volumeStore';
	import { crosshairSlice } from '$lib/stores/crosshairSlice';
	import { statusStore } from '$lib/stores/statusStore';
	import OrthogonalViewer from '../OrthogonalViewer.svelte';
	import type { VolumeMeta } from '$lib/geometry/types';
	import type { LayerSpec } from '@brainflow/api';

	// Props
	let { 
		glContainer, 
		initialState,
		componentState
	}: { 
		glContainer?: ComponentContainer; 
		initialState?: { layerId?: string | null };
		componentState?: { layerId?: string | null };
	} = $props();

	// State
	let layerId = $state(componentState?.layerId ?? initialState?.layerId ?? null);
	let containerElement = $state<HTMLDivElement>();
	let containerSize = $state({ width: 0, height: 0 });
	let isDragOver = $state(false);
	let volumeMeta: VolumeMeta | null = $state(null);
	let layers: LayerSpec[] = $state([]);

	console.log('VolumeView created with:', { componentState, initialState, layerId });

	// Get the first layer if no layerId is set
	const layerStore = useLayerStore.getState();
	
	// Subscribe to layer store changes
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = useLayerStore.subscribe((state) => {
			console.log('VolumeView: Layer store updated, layers:', state.layers.length);
			
			// If we don't have a layerId and there are layers available
			if (!layerId && state.layers.length > 0) {
				// Get the first volume layer
				const firstLayer = state.layers.find(l => l.spec && 'Volume' in l.spec);
				if (firstLayer && 'Volume' in firstLayer.spec) {
					layerId = firstLayer.spec.Volume.id;
					console.log('VolumeView: Auto-selected first layer:', layerId);
					// Update the title
					if (glContainer) {
						glContainer.setTitle(`Volume View - ${layerId}`);
					}
				}
			}
			
			// If we're showing an empty view and a new layer was added, switch to it
			if (!layerId && state.layers.length > 0) {
				const latestLayer = state.layers[state.layers.length - 1];
				if (latestLayer.spec && 'Volume' in latestLayer.spec) {
					layerId = latestLayer.spec.Volume.id;
					console.log('VolumeView: Switched to latest layer:', layerId);
					// Update the title
					if (glContainer) {
						glContainer.setTitle(`Volume View - ${layerId}`);
					}
				}
			}
			
			// Debug: print all layers and their GPU status
			state.layers.forEach((layer, idx) => {
				console.log(`VolumeView: Layer[${idx}]:`, {
					id: 'Volume' in layer.spec ? layer.spec.Volume.id : 'unknown',
					hasGpu: !!layer.gpu,
					gpuDims: layer.gpu && 'dim' in layer.gpu ? layer.gpu.dim : 'no dims',
					isLoading: layer.isLoadingGpu,
					error: layer.error
				});
			});
		});
		
		return unsubscribe;
	});

	// Get volume metadata when layer changes
	function updateVolumeMetadata() {
		if (layerId) {
			const layerEntry = useLayerStore.getState().layers.find(l => 
				l.spec && 'Volume' in l.spec && l.spec.Volume.id === layerId
			);
			
			if (layerEntry && layerEntry.gpu && 'dim' in layerEntry.gpu) {
				const gpu = layerEntry.gpu;
				console.log('VolumeView: Found GPU info for layer', layerId, gpu);
				// Create VolumeMeta from GPU info
				volumeMeta = {
					dims: { x: gpu.dim[0], y: gpu.dim[1], z: gpu.dim[2] },
					spacing: { x: gpu.spacing[0], y: gpu.spacing[1], z: gpu.spacing[2] },
					origin: { x: gpu.origin[0], y: gpu.origin[1], z: gpu.origin[2] }
				};
				
				// Get all layers with the same GPU resources
				layers = useLayerStore.getState().layers
					.filter(l => l.gpu) // Only include layers with GPU resources
					.map(l => l.spec);
			} else {
				console.log('VolumeView: No GPU info found for layer', layerId);
				volumeMeta = null;
				layers = [];
			}
		} else {
			volumeMeta = null;
			layers = [];
		}
	}
	
	// Update when layerId changes
	$effect(() => {
		updateVolumeMetadata();
	});
	
	// Also update when layer store changes
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = useLayerStore.subscribe(() => {
			updateVolumeMetadata();
		});
		
		return unsubscribe;
	});
	
	// Handle mouse world coordinate updates
	function handleMouseWorldCoord(coords: [number, number, number] | null) {
		statusStore.setMouseWorldCoord(coords);
	}

	// Container resize handling
	let resizeObserver: ResizeObserver | null = null;

	function handleContainerResize(width: number, height: number) {
		if (width > 0 && height > 0) {
			containerSize = { width, height };
			// TODO: Notify backend about overall container resize
		}
	}

	// Drag and drop handlers
	function handleDragOver(event: DragEvent) {
		event.preventDefault();
		if (event.dataTransfer) {
			event.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy';
		}
		isDragOver = true;
	}

	function handleDragEnter(event: DragEvent) {
		event.preventDefault();
		isDragOver = true;
	}

	function handleDragLeave(event: DragEvent) {
		event.preventDefault();
		isDragOver = false;
	}

	async function handleDrop(event: DragEvent) {
		event.preventDefault();
		isDragOver = false;
		
		console.log('🎯 Drop event received in VolumeView');
		
		if (!event.dataTransfer) {
			console.error('❌ No dataTransfer in drop event');
			return;
		}
		
		// Log all available data formats for debugging
		const formats = event.dataTransfer.types;
		console.log('📋 Available data formats:', formats);
		
		const fileData = event.dataTransfer.getData('application/x-brainflow-file');
		const fallbackData = event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
		
		console.log('📦 File data:', fileData);
		console.log('📦 Fallback data:', fallbackData);
		
		const dataToUse = fileData || fallbackData;
		
		if (dataToUse) {
			try {
				const { path, name } = JSON.parse(dataToUse);
				console.log('✅ Dropped file:', name, 'from', path);
				
				// Load the file
				const handleInfo = await coreApi.load_file(path);
				console.log('File loaded via drag-drop:', handleInfo);
				
				// Add to volume store
				useVolumeStore.getState().add(handleInfo);

				// Create a new layer
				const newLayerId = `layer-${nanoid(5)}`;
				const defaultLayerSpec: LayerSpec = {
					Volume: {
						id: newLayerId,
						source_resource_id: handleInfo.id,
						colormap: 'grayscale',
						slice_axis: null,
						slice_index: null
					}
				};
				
				// Add layer and request GPU resources
				useLayerStore.getState().addLayer(defaultLayerSpec);
				useLayerStore.getState().requestGpuResources(newLayerId);
				
				// Update this view to show the new layer
				layerId = newLayerId;
				
				// Update the title if we have a container
				if (glContainer) {
					glContainer.setTitle(name);
				}
			} catch (error) {
				console.error('Failed to load dropped file:', error);
			}
		}
	}

	// GoldenLayout integration
	$effect(() => {
		if (glContainer) {
			// Update title
			glContainer.setTitle(`Volume View${layerId ? ` - ${layerId}` : ''}`);
			
			// Handle state changes
			const handleStateChanged = () => {
				const newState = glContainer.getState() as { layerId?: string | null };
				console.log('VolumeView state changed:', newState);
				if (newState?.layerId !== layerId) {
					layerId = newState?.layerId ?? null;
					console.log('VolumeView layerId updated to:', layerId);
				}
			};
			
			glContainer.on('stateChanged', handleStateChanged);
			
			// Also provide a method to update state from outside
			(glContainer as any).updateLayerId = (newLayerId: string) => {
				console.log('VolumeView updateLayerId called with:', newLayerId);
				layerId = newLayerId;
				glContainer.setState({ layerId: newLayerId });
			};
			
			return () => {
				glContainer.off('stateChanged', handleStateChanged);
			};
		}
	});

	// Lifecycle
	onMount(() => {
		// Check for existing layers on mount
		console.log('VolumeView: Mounted, checking for existing layers...');
		const currentState = useLayerStore.getState();
		if (currentState.layers.length > 0) {
			console.log('VolumeView: Found existing layers on mount:', currentState.layers.length);
			// Trigger metadata update
			updateVolumeMetadata();
		}
		
		if (containerElement) {
			resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver((entries) => {
				const entry = entries[0];
				const { width, height } = entry.contentRect;
				handleContainerResize(width, height);
			});
			resizeObserver.observe(containerElement);
		}
	});

	onDestroy(() => {
		resizeObserver?.disconnect();
	});
</script>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/BridgeExplorer.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
    import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
    import { bridgeLogger, loggedCoreApi, type BridgeLogEntry } from '../bridgeLogger';
    import type { LayerSpec } from '../api';

    // Command definitions with pre-filled test data
    const commands = [
        {
            name: 'load_file',
            description: 'Load a NIfTI/GIfTI file',
            params: [
                { name: 'path', type: 'string', default: '/Users/bbuchsbaum/code/brainflow2/test-data/unit/toy_t1w.nii.gz' }
            ]
        },
        {
            name: 'supports_webgpu',
            description: 'Check if WebGPU is supported',
            params: []
        },
        {
            name: 'fs_list_directory',
            description: 'List directory contents',
            params: [
                { name: 'dir', type: 'string', default: '/Users/bbuchsbaum/code/brainflow2/test-data' }
            ]
        },
        {
            name: 'world_to_voxel',
            description: 'Convert world to voxel coordinates',
            params: [
                { name: 'volume_id', type: 'string', default: 'volume-123' },
                { name: 'world_coord', type: 'array', default: '[10.5, 20.3, 30.1]' }
            ]
        },
        {
            name: 'set_crosshair',
            description: 'Set crosshair position',
            params: [
                { name: 'coords', type: 'array', default: '[100, 150, 75]' }
            ]
        },
        {
            name: 'set_frame_params',
            description: 'Set frame parameters',
            params: [
                { name: 'origin', type: 'array', default: '[0, 0, 0, 1]' },
                { name: 'u_basis', type: 'array', default: '[1, 0, 0, 0]' },
                { name: 'v_basis', type: 'array', default: '[0, 1, 0, 0]' }
            ]
        },
        {
            name: 'request_layer_gpu_resources',
            description: 'Request GPU resources for a layer',
            params: [
                { name: 'layer_spec', type: 'object', default: '{"type": "Volume", "id": "layer-1", "source_resource_id": "volume-123", "colormap": "grayscale"}' }
            ]
        }
    ];

    let selectedCommand = commands[0];
    let paramValues: Record<string, string> = {};
    let logs: BridgeLogEntry[] = [];
    let isExecuting = false;
    let result: any = null;
    let error: any = null;

    // Initialize param values
    function initParamValues() {
        paramValues = {};
        selectedCommand.params.forEach(param => {
            paramValues[param.name] = param.default || '';
        });
    }

    // Parse parameter value based on type
    function parseParamValue(value: string, type: string): any {
        switch (type) {
            case 'array':
                return JSON.parse(value);
            case 'object':
                return JSON.parse(value);
            case 'number':
                return Number(value);
            case 'boolean':
                return value === 'true';
            default:
                return value;
        }
    }

    // Execute the selected command
    async function executeCommand() {
        isExecuting = true;
        result = null;
        error = null;

        try {
            const args = selectedCommand.params.map(param => 
                parseParamValue(paramValues[param.name], param.type)
            );

            const fn = (loggedCoreApi as any)[selectedCommand.name];
            if (!fn) {
                throw new Error(`Command ${selectedCommand.name} not found`);
            }

            result = await fn(...args);
        } catch (err) {
            error = err;
        } finally {
            isExecuting = false;
        }
    }

    // Subscribe to logs
    let unsubscribe: (() => void) | null = null;

    onMount(() => {
        bridgeLogger.enable();
        logs = bridgeLogger.getLogs();
        unsubscribe = bridgeLogger.onLog((log) => {
            logs = [...logs, log];
            if (logs.length > 50) {
                logs = logs.slice(-50);
            }
        });
        initParamValues();
    });

    onDestroy(() => {
        if (unsubscribe) {
            unsubscribe();
        }
    });

    $: if (selectedCommand) {
        initParamValues();
    }
</script>

<div class="bridge-explorer">
    <h2>🔌 Bridge Command Explorer</h2>
    
    <div class="command-section">

        <p class="description">{selectedCommand.description}</p>

</div>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/BridgeLogViewer.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
    import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
    import { bridgeLogger, type BridgeLogEntry } from '../bridgeLogger';

    let logs: BridgeLogEntry[] = [];
    let filter = '';
    let autoScroll = true;
    let logContainer: HTMLDivElement;
    let isEnabled = false;

    // Filter logs
    $: filteredLogs = logs.filter(log => {
        if (!filter) return true;
        const searchStr = filter.toLowerCase();
        return log.command.toLowerCase().includes(searchStr) ||
               JSON.stringify(log.params).toLowerCase().includes(searchStr) ||
               JSON.stringify(log.result || log.error).toLowerCase().includes(searchStr);
    });

    // Subscribe to logs
    let unsubscribe: (() => void) | null = null;

    onMount(() => {
        logs = bridgeLogger.getLogs();
        unsubscribe = bridgeLogger.onLog((log) => {
            logs = [...logs, log];
            if (autoScroll && logContainer) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    logContainer.scrollTop = logContainer.scrollHeight;
                }, 10);
            }
        });
    });

    onDestroy(() => {
        if (unsubscribe) {
            unsubscribe();
        }
    });

    function clearLogs() {
        bridgeLogger.clear();
        logs = [];
    }

    function toggleLogging() {
        if (isEnabled) {
            bridgeLogger.disable();
            isEnabled = false;
        } else {
            bridgeLogger.enable();
            isEnabled = true;
        }
    }

    function formatDuration(ms?: number): string {
        if (!ms) return '';
        if (ms < 1000) return `${ms}ms`;
        return `${(ms / 1000).toFixed(2)}s`;
    }

    function formatTime(timestamp: number): string {
        const date = new Date(timestamp);
        return date.toLocaleTimeString();
    }
</script>

<div class="log-viewer">
    <div class="header">
        <h3>📊 Bridge Log Viewer</h3>
        <div class="controls">
            <input 
                type="text" 
                placeholder="Filter logs..." 
                bind:value={filter}
                class="filter-input"
            />
            <label>
                <input type="checkbox" bind:checked={autoScroll} />
                Auto-scroll
            </label>
            <button on:click={toggleLogging} class="toggle-btn">
                {isEnabled ? 'Disable' : 'Enable'} Logging
            </button>
            <button on:click={clearLogs} class="clear-btn">Clear</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="log-container" bind:this={logContainer}>
        {#if filteredLogs.length === 0}
            <div class="empty">No logs to display</div>
        {:else}
            {#each filteredLogs as log, i}
                <div class="log-entry {log.error ? 'error' : 'success'}">
                    <div class="log-header">
                        <span class="index">#{i + 1}</span>
                        <span class="time">{formatTime(log.timestamp)}</span>
                        <span class="command">{log.command}</span>
                        <span class="duration">{formatDuration(log.duration)}</span>
                        <span class="status">{log.error ? '❌' : '✅'}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <details>
                        <summary>Parameters</summary>
                        <pre class="params">{JSON.stringify(log.params, null, 2)}</pre>
                    </details>
                    
                    {#if log.result !== undefined}
                        <details>
                            <summary>Result</summary>
                            <pre class="result">{JSON.stringify(log.result, null, 2)}</pre>
                        </details>
                    {/if}
                    
                    {#if log.error}
                        <details open>
                            <summary>Error</summary>
                            <pre class="error-details">{JSON.stringify(log.error, null, 2)}</pre>
                        </details>
                    {/if}
                </div>
            {/each}
        {/if}
    </div>
</div>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/MountableTreeBrowser.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	import { getContext, tick, onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
	import type { ComponentContainer } from 'golden-layout';
	import { getGlContainer } from '$lib/layout/glUtils';
	import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import { useVolumeStore } from '$lib/stores/volumeStore';
	import { useLayerStore } from '$lib/stores/layerStore';
	import { mountStore, useMountStore, FILE_PATTERNS, type FilePatternKey } from '$lib/stores/mountStore';
	import { nanoid } from 'nanoid';
	import type { LayerSpec, FlatNode, TreePayload } from '$lib/api';
	import { listen } from '@tauri-apps/api/event';
	import { invoke } from '@tauri-apps/api/core';
	import { waitForTauri } from '$lib/tauri-ready';
	import FileIcon from '$lib/components/icons/FileIcon.svelte';
	import { RefreshCw, Filter, X, ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Folder } from 'lucide-svelte';

	// --- Component State ---
	let container: ComponentContainer | undefined;
	let isLoading = $state(false);
	let errorMsg: string | null = $state(null);
	let treeNodesMap = $state(new Map<string, FlatNode[]>()); // Map mount ID to nodes
	let nodeMapByMount = $state(new Map<string, Map<string, FlatNode>>()); // Map mount ID to node map
	let childrenMapByMount = $state(new Map<string, Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>>()); // Map mount ID to children map
	
	// Mount store subscriptions
	let mounts = $state(useMountStore().getAllMounts());
	let activeMountId = $state(useMountStore().activeMountId);
	
	// Subscribe to store changes
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = mountStore.subscribe((state) => {
			const newMounts = state.getAllMounts();
			console.log('📊 Mount store updated. Mounts:', newMounts.length, newMounts.map(m => ({ id: m.id, path: m.path })));
			mounts = newMounts;
			activeMountId = state.activeMountId;
		});
		
		// Log initial state
		console.log('📊 Initial mounts:', mounts.length, mounts.map(m => ({ id: m.id, path: m.path })));
		
		return unsubscribe;
	});
	
	// File filter dialog state
	let showFilterDialog = $state(false);
	let filterDialogMountId: string | null = $state(null);
	let selectedPatterns: string[] = $state([]);
	
	// Selection state
	let selectedNodeId: string | null = $state(null);
	
	// Click handling state for distinguishing single/double clicks
	let clickTimeouts = new Map<string, number>();

	// --- Effects ---
	let unlistenMount: (() => void) | null = null;
	
	// Setup event listener in a separate effect to ensure it's always active
	$effect(() => {
		let localUnlisten: (() => void) | null = null;
		
		(async () => {
			// Wait for Tauri to be ready
			await waitForTauri();
			
			// Listen for mount directory events from the native menu
			try {
				console.log('🔧 Setting up mount-directory-event listener...');
				localUnlisten = await listen('mount-directory-event', async (event: any) => {
					console.log('🔔 Received mount directory event:', event);
					const path = event.payload?.path;
					if (path) {
						console.log('📁 Processing mount directory path:', path);
						await handleMountFromMenu(path);
					} else {
						console.error('❌ No path in mount directory event payload:', event.payload);
					}
				});
				console.log('✅ Mount directory event listener registered successfully');
				unlistenMount = localUnlisten;
			} catch (error) {
				console.error('❌ Failed to register mount directory event listener:', error);
			}
		})();
		
		// Cleanup function
		return () => {
			if (localUnlisten) {
				console.log('🧹 Cleaning up mount directory event listener');
				localUnlisten();
			}
		};
	});
	
	onMount(async () => {
		container = getGlContainer();
		
		await tick();
		console.log("MountableTreeBrowser initialized.");
		
		// Mount default directory if no mounts exist
		if (mounts.length === 0) {
			const defaultPath = "/Users/bbuchsbaum/code/brainflow2/test-data";
			useMountStore().mountDirectory(defaultPath, "Test Data");
		}
		
		// Load initial directories for all mounts
		for (const mount of mounts) {
			loadDirectory(mount.id, mount.path);
		}
	});
	
	onDestroy(() => {
		if (unlistenMount) {
			unlistenMount();
		}
	});

	// Rebuild maps whenever tree nodes change for a mount
	function rebuildMapsForMount(mountId: string, nodes: FlatNode[]) {
		console.log(`Rebuilding tree maps for mount ${mountId}...`);
		const newNodes = new Map<string, FlatNode>();
		const newChildren = new Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>();
		newChildren.set(null, []); // Initialize root children

		for (const [index, node] of nodes.entries()) {
			newNodes.set(node.id, node);
			const parentId = node.parent_idx !== null && node.parent_idx !== undefined && node.parent_idx < nodes.length 
				? nodes[node.parent_idx].id 
				: null;

			if (!newChildren.has(parentId)) {
				newChildren.set(parentId, []);
			}
			newChildren.get(parentId)!.push(node);
		}
		
		// Sort children alphabetically (directories first, then files)
		for (const children of newChildren.values()) {
			children.sort((a, b) => {
				if (a.is_dir !== b.is_dir) {
					return a.is_dir ? -1 : 1; // Directories first
				}
				return a.name.localeCompare(b.name); // Then alphabetical
			});
		}

		nodeMapByMount.set(mountId, newNodes);
		childrenMapByMount.set(mountId, newChildren);
		console.log(`Tree maps rebuilt for mount ${mountId}.`);
	}

	// --- Event Handlers ---
	let showMountDialog = $state(false);
	let mountPath = $state('');
	
	// Handle mount from native menu
	async function handleMountFromMenu(path: string) {
		console.log('📍 handleMountFromMenu called with path:', path);
		try {
			const label = path.split('/').pop() || path;
			console.log('📍 Creating mount with label:', label);
			const mountId = useMountStore().mountDirectory(path, label);
			console.log('📍 Mount created with ID:', mountId);
			await loadDirectory(mountId, path);
			console.log('📍 Directory loaded successfully');
			
			// Update dynamic menus with current mounts
			await updateDynamicMenus();
			console.log('📍 Dynamic menus updated');
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ Error mounting directory from menu:", error);
			errorMsg = "Failed to mount directory";
		}
	}
	
	// Update the backend menus with current state
	async function updateDynamicMenus() {
		const currentMounts = mounts.map(m => ({
			id: m.id,
			path: m.path
		}));
		
		try {
			await invoke('update_dynamic_menus', { mounted: currentMounts });
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("Failed to update dynamic menus:", error);
		}
	}
	
	function handleMountDirectory() {
		showMountDialog = true;
		mountPath = '';
	}
	
	async function confirmMount() {
		if (!mountPath) return;
		
		try {
			const label = mountPath.split('/').pop() || mountPath;
			const mountId = useMountStore().mountDirectory(mountPath, label);
			await loadDirectory(mountId, mountPath);
			showMountDialog = false;
			mountPath = '';
			
			// Update dynamic menus
			await updateDynamicMenus();
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("Error mounting directory:", error);
			errorMsg = "Failed to mount directory";
		}
	}

	async function loadDirectory(mountId: string, dir: string) {
		if (isLoading) return;
		isLoading = true;
		errorMsg = null;
		
		console.log(`Loading directory for mount ${mountId}: ${dir}`);
		try {
			const payload = await coreApi.fs_list_directory(dir);
			await tick();
			
			// Filter nodes based on mount's file patterns
			const mount = useMountStore().getMountById(mountId);
			let filteredNodes = payload.nodes;
			
			if (mount && mount.filePatterns.length > 0) {
				filteredNodes = payload.nodes.filter(node => {
					if (node.is_dir) return true; // Always show directories
					
					// Check if file matches any of the patterns
					const lowerName = node.name.toLowerCase();
					return mount.filePatterns.some(pattern => {
						if (pattern.endsWith('.gz') && lowerName.endsWith('.gz')) {
							// Special handling for .nii.gz files
							const basePattern = pattern.slice(0, -3); // Remove .gz
							return lowerName.endsWith(pattern) || 
								   (lowerName.endsWith('.gz') && lowerName.slice(0, -3).endsWith(basePattern));
						}
						return lowerName.endsWith(pattern);
					});
				});
			}
			
			treeNodesMap.set(mountId, filteredNodes);
			rebuildMapsForMount(mountId, filteredNodes);
			console.log(`Loaded ${filteredNodes.length} nodes for mount ${mountId}.`);
		} catch (error: any) {
			console.error(`Error listing directory ${dir}: ${JSON.stringify(error)}`);
			errorMsg = error?.message || 'Failed to list directory.';
			treeNodesMap.set(mountId, []);
		} finally {
			isLoading = false;
		}
	}

	function handleNodeClick(mountId: string, node: FlatNode) {
		if (node.is_dir) {
			console.log(`Directory clicked: ${node.id}`);
			loadDirectory(mountId, node.id);
		} else {
			// Single click - just select the file, don't load it
			console.log(`File selected: ${node.id}`);
			selectedNodeId = node.id;
		}
	}

	function handleNodeDoubleClick(mountId: string, node: FlatNode) {
		console.log(`Node double-clicked:`, node);
		if (!node.is_dir) {
			console.log(`File double-clicked: ${node.id}`);
			handleSingleFile(node.id, node.name);
		} else {
			console.log(`Directory double-clicked: ${node.id}`);
		}
	}

	async function handleSingleFile(fullPath: string, fileName: string) {
		if (isLoading) return;
		isLoading = true;
		errorMsg = null;

		try {
			console.log(`Loading file: ${fileName} from path: ${fullPath}`);
			const handleInfo = await coreApi.load_file(fullPath);
			console.log('File loaded successfully:', handleInfo);
			
			useVolumeStore.getState().add(handleInfo);

			const layerId = `layer-${nanoid(5)}`;
			const defaultLayerSpec: LayerSpec = {
				Volume: {
					id: layerId,
					source_resource_id: handleInfo.id,
					colormap: 'grayscale',
					slice_axis: null,
					slice_index: null
				}
			};
			console.log('Adding default layer spec:', defaultLayerSpec);
			useLayerStore.getState().addLayer(defaultLayerSpec);
			useLayerStore.getState().requestGpuResources(layerId);

			// The VolumeView will automatically pick up the new layer through the store subscription
			console.log('Layer added, VolumeView should update automatically');

		} catch (error: unknown) {
			console.error(`Error loading file ${fileName}:`, error);
			let message = `Failed to load ${fileName}.`;
			if (error instanceof Error) {
				message = error.message;
			} else if (typeof error === 'string') {
				message = error;
			} else if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'message' in error) {
				message = String((error as any).message);
			}
			errorMsg = message;
		} finally {
			isLoading = false;
		}
	}

	function showFilterDialogForMount(mountId: string) {
		const mount = useMountStore().getMountById(mountId);
		if (mount) {
			filterDialogMountId = mountId;
			selectedPatterns = [...mount.filePatterns];
			showFilterDialog = true;
		}
	}

	function applyFilters() {
		if (filterDialogMountId) {
			useMountStore().updateMountPatterns(filterDialogMountId, selectedPatterns);
			const mount = useMountStore().getMountById(filterDialogMountId);
			if (mount) {
				loadDirectory(filterDialogMountId, mount.path);
			}
		}
		showFilterDialog = false;
		filterDialogMountId = null;
	}

	function togglePattern(pattern: string) {
		const index = selectedPatterns.indexOf(pattern);
		if (index >= 0) {
			selectedPatterns = selectedPatterns.filter(p => p !== pattern);
		} else {
			selectedPatterns = [...selectedPatterns, pattern];
		}
	}

	function selectPreset(key: FilePatternKey) {
		selectedPatterns = [...FILE_PATTERNS[key]];
	}
	
	// Svelte action for handling click/double-click intelligently
	function clickHandler(node: HTMLElement, params: { mountId: string, treeNode: FlatNode }) {
		const DOUBLE_CLICK_DELAY = 300; // ms
		
		function handleClick(event: MouseEvent) {
			event.preventDefault();
			
			const nodeId = params.treeNode.id;
			const existingTimeout = clickTimeouts.get(nodeId);
			
			if (existingTimeout) {
				// This is a double-click
				clearTimeout(existingTimeout);
				clickTimeouts.delete(nodeId);
				console.log(`Double-click detected on: ${params.treeNode.name}`);
				handleNodeDoubleClick(params.mountId, params.treeNode);
			} else {
				// First click - wait to see if it's a double-click
				const timeoutId = window.setTimeout(() => {
					clickTimeouts.delete(nodeId);
					console.log(`Single-click confirmed on: ${params.treeNode.name}`);
					handleNodeClick(params.mountId, params.treeNode);
				}, DOUBLE_CLICK_DELAY);
				
				clickTimeouts.set(nodeId, timeoutId);
			}
		}
		
		node.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
		
		return {
			destroy() {
				node.removeEventListener('click', handleClick);
				// Clean up any pending timeouts
				const nodeId = params.treeNode.id;
				const timeout = clickTimeouts.get(nodeId);
				if (timeout) {
					clearTimeout(timeout);
					clickTimeouts.delete(nodeId);
				}
			}
		};
	}


	// Handle drag start for files
	function handleDragStart(event: DragEvent, node: FlatNode) {
		console.log('🎯 Drag start event fired for:', node.name, 'is_dir:', node.is_dir);
		
		if (node.is_dir) {
			console.log('❌ Cannot drag directories');
			event.preventDefault();
			return;
		}
		
		if (!event.dataTransfer) {
			console.error('❌ No dataTransfer available');
			return;
		}
		
		// Set drag data
		event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'copy';
		const data = JSON.stringify({
			path: node.id,
			name: node.name
		});
		
		try {
			event.dataTransfer.setData('application/x-brainflow-file', data);
			event.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', data); // Fallback
			console.log('✅ Drag data set successfully:', data);
			
			// Add visual feedback
			if (event.target instanceof HTMLElement) {
				event.target.style.opacity = '0.5';
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error('❌ Failed to set drag data:', error);
		}
	}
	
	// Handle drag end to reset visual feedback
	function handleDragEnd(event: DragEvent) {
		if (event.target instanceof HTMLElement) {
			event.target.style.opacity = '';
		}
		console.log('🎯 Drag ended');
	}
</script>

<!-- Recursive Tree Node Component -->
{#snippet renderChildren(mountId: string, parentId: string | null, level: number = 0)}
	{@const childrenMap = childrenMapByMount.get(mountId)}
	{@const children = childrenMap?.get(parentId)}
	{#if children && children.length > 0}
		<ul class="tree-list" style="padding-left: {level > 0 ? '1.25rem' : '0'}">
			{#each children as node (node.id)}
				{@const typedNode = node as FlatNode}
				<li 
					class="tree-item {selectedNodeId === typedNode.id ? 'selected' : ''}"
					use:clickHandler={{ mountId, treeNode: typedNode }}
					onkeydown={(e) => {
						if (e.key === 'Enter') {
							e.preventDefault();
							handleNodeDoubleClick(mountId, typedNode);
						}
					}}
					draggable={!typedNode.is_dir}
					ondragstart={(e) => handleDragStart(e, typedNode)}
					ondragend={handleDragEnd}
					role="treeitem"
					tabindex="0"
					title={typedNode.id}
				>
					<div class="tree-item-content">
						<FileIcon 
							fileName={typedNode.name} 
							isDirectory={typedNode.is_dir}
							isOpen={false}
							class="tree-icon"
						/>
						<span class="tree-label">{typedNode.name}</span>
					</div>
					{#if typedNode.is_dir}
						{@render renderChildren(mountId, typedNode.id, level + 1)}
					{/if}
				</li>
			{/each}
		</ul>
	{/if}
{/snippet}

<div class="tree-browser-container">
	{#if false}
	<!-- Keeping mount button code for reference, but using native menu instead -->
	<div class="toolbar">
		<button onclick={handleMountDirectory} class="toolbar-button">
			Mount Directory
		</button>
	</div>
	{/if}

	{#if errorMsg}
		<div class="feedback error">Error: {errorMsg}</div>
	{/if}

	<div class="mounts-container">
		{#if mounts.length === 0}
			<div class="empty-state">
				<p>No directories mounted</p>
				<p>Use <strong>File → Mount Directory...</strong> to add a folder</p>
				<p style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #999; margin-top: 20px;">
					Component ready • Event listener: {unlistenMount ? '✅' : '⏳'}
				</p>
			</div>
		{:else}
			{#each mounts as mount (mount.id)}
				{@const nodes = treeNodesMap.get(mount.id) || []}
				{@const isActive = mount.id === activeMountId}
				<div class="mount-section" class:active={isActive}>
					<div class="mount-header">
						<button 
							class="expand-button"
							onclick={() => useMountStore().toggleMountExpanded(mount.id)}
							aria-label={mount.isExpanded ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'}
						>
							{#if mount.isExpanded}
								<ChevronDown size={16} />
							{:else}
								<ChevronRight size={16} />
							{/if}
						</button>
						<Folder class="mount-folder-icon" size={16} />
						<span 
							class="mount-label" 
							onclick={() => useMountStore().setActiveMountId(mount.id)}
							onkeydown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && useMountStore().setActiveMountId(mount.id)}
							role="button"
							tabindex="0"
							title={mount.path}
						>
							{mount.label}
						</span>
						<div class="mount-actions">
							<button 
								class="icon-button" 
								onclick={() => showFilterDialogForMount(mount.id)}
								title="Configure file filters"
								aria-label="Configure file filters"
							>
								<Filter size={16} />
							</button>
							<button 
								class="icon-button" 
								onclick={() => loadDirectory(mount.id, mount.path)}
								title="Refresh"
								aria-label="Refresh directory"
							>
								<RefreshCw size={16} />
							</button>
							<button 
								class="icon-button icon-button-danger" 
								onclick={async () => {
									useMountStore().unmountDirectory(mount.id);
									await updateDynamicMenus();
								}}
								title="Unmount"
								aria-label="Unmount directory"
							>
								<X size={16} />
							</button>
						</div>
					</div>
					
					{#if mount.isExpanded}
						<div class="tree-view">
							{#if isLoading && isActive}
								<p>Loading...</p>
							{:else if nodes.length > 0}
								{@render renderChildren(mount.id, null)}
							{:else}
								<p>No matching files found</p>
							{/if}
						</div>
					{/if}
				</div>
			{/each}
		{/if}
	</div>
</div>

<!-- Mount Dialog -->
{#if showMountDialog}
	<div class="dialog-overlay" onclick={() => showMountDialog = false}>
		<div class="dialog" onclick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
			<h3>Mount Directory</h3>
			<div class="mount-form">
				<label>
					Directory Path:
					<input 
						type="text" 
						bind:value={mountPath}
						placeholder="/path/to/directory"
						class="mount-input"
						onkeydown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && confirmMount()}
					/>
				</label>
			</div>
			<div class="dialog-actions">
				<button onclick={() => showMountDialog = false} class="cancel-button">Cancel</button>
				<button onclick={confirmMount} class="apply-button" disabled={!mountPath}>Mount</button>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
{/if}

<!-- Filter Dialog -->
{#if showFilterDialog}
	<div class="dialog-overlay" onclick={() => showFilterDialog = false}>
		<div class="dialog" onclick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
			<h3>Configure File Filters</h3>
			
			<div class="filter-presets">
				<h4>Presets:</h4>
				<button onclick={() => selectPreset('nifti')} class="preset-button">NIfTI</button>
				<button onclick={() => selectPreset('gifti')} class="preset-button">GIfTI</button>
				<button onclick={() => selectPreset('image')} class="preset-button">Images</button>
				<button onclick={() => selectPreset('data')} class="preset-button">Data</button>
				<button onclick={() => selectPreset('all')} class="preset-button">All Files</button>
			</div>
			
			<div class="filter-patterns">
				<h4>File Extensions:</h4>
				<div class="pattern-grid">
					{#each ['.nii', '.nii.gz', '.gii', '.gii.gz', '.png', '.jpg', '.csv', '.tsv'] as pattern}
						<label class="pattern-checkbox">
							<input 
								type="checkbox" 
								checked={selectedPatterns.includes(pattern)}
								onchange={() => togglePattern(pattern)}
							/>
							{pattern}
						</label>
					{/each}
				</div>
			</div>
			
			<div class="dialog-actions">
				<button onclick={() => showFilterDialog = false} class="cancel-button">Cancel</button>
				<button onclick={applyFilters} class="apply-button">Apply</button>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
{/if}

		bottom: 0;
		background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/OrthogonalViewer.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
  import { createEventDispatcher } from 'svelte';
  import SliceViewer from './SliceViewer.svelte';
  import type { VolumeMeta, Vec3 } from '../geometry/types';
  import type { LayerSpec } from '@brainflow/api';
  
  // Props
  export let volumeMeta: VolumeMeta;
  export let layers: LayerSpec[] = [];
  export let layout: 'horizontal' | 'vertical' | 'grid' = 'grid';
  export let viewSize = 256; // Deprecated, use width/height instead
  export let width: number | null = null;
  export let height: number | null = null;
  export let showCrosshair = true;
  export let showLabels = true;
  export let showSliders = true;
  export let onMouseWorldCoord: ((coords: [number, number, number] | null) => void) | null = null;
  
  // State
  let crosshair: Vec3 = {
    x: volumeMeta.origin.x + (volumeMeta.dims.x * volumeMeta.spacing.x) / 2,
    y: volumeMeta.origin.y + (volumeMeta.dims.y * volumeMeta.spacing.y) / 2,
    z: volumeMeta.origin.z + (volumeMeta.dims.z * volumeMeta.spacing.z) / 2
  };
  
  // Convert world position to slice indices
  $: axialSlice = Math.round((crosshair.z - volumeMeta.origin.z) / volumeMeta.spacing.z);
  $: coronalSlice = Math.round((crosshair.y - volumeMeta.origin.y) / volumeMeta.spacing.y);
  $: sagittalSlice = Math.round((crosshair.x - volumeMeta.origin.x) / volumeMeta.spacing.x);
  
  // Calculate view sizes based on layout
  $: containerWidth = width || viewSize * 2;
  $: containerHeight = height || viewSize * 2;
  
  // For grid layout: axial gets half width, coronal/sagittal share the other half
  $: axialWidth = layout === 'grid' ? Math.floor((containerWidth - 12) / 2) : viewSize;
  $: axialHeight = layout === 'grid' ? containerHeight - 16 : viewSize;
  $: coronalWidth = layout === 'grid' ? Math.floor((containerWidth - 12) / 2) : viewSize;
  $: coronalHeight = layout === 'grid' ? Math.floor((containerHeight - 16) / 2) : viewSize;
  $: sagittalWidth = layout === 'grid' ? Math.floor((containerWidth - 12) / 2) : viewSize;
  $: sagittalHeight = layout === 'grid' ? Math.floor((containerHeight - 16) / 2) : viewSize;
  
  const dispatch = createEventDispatcher();
  
  function handleCrosshairChange(newPos: Vec3) {
    crosshair = newPos;
    dispatch('crosshairChange', { position: newPos });
  }
  
  function handleAxialSliceChange(index: number) {
    crosshair = {
      ...crosshair,
      z: volumeMeta.origin.z + index * volumeMeta.spacing.z
    };
    dispatch('sliceChange', { plane: 'axial', index });
  }
  
  function handleCoronalSliceChange(index: number) {
    crosshair = {
      ...crosshair,
      y: volumeMeta.origin.y + index * volumeMeta.spacing.y
    };
    dispatch('sliceChange', { plane: 'coronal', index });
  }
  
  function handleSagittalSliceChange(index: number) {
    crosshair = {
      ...crosshair,
      x: volumeMeta.origin.x + index * volumeMeta.spacing.x
    };
    dispatch('sliceChange', { plane: 'sagittal', index });
  }
  
  // Layout classes
  $: layoutClass = {
    horizontal: 'orthogonal-horizontal',
    vertical: 'orthogonal-vertical',
    grid: 'orthogonal-grid'
  }[layout];
</script>

<div class="orthogonal-viewer {layoutClass}">
  <div class="view-container">
    {#if showLabels}
      <div class="view-label">Axial (Z={axialSlice})</div>
    {/if}
    <SliceViewer
      {volumeMeta}
      plane="axial"
      sliceIndex={axialSlice}
      {layers}
      {crosshair}
      {showCrosshair}
      showSlider={showSliders}
      onCrosshairChange={handleCrosshairChange}
      onSliceChange={handleAxialSliceChange}
      {onMouseWorldCoord}
      width={axialWidth}
      height={axialHeight}
    />
  </div>
  
  <div class="view-container">
    {#if showLabels}
      <div class="view-label">Coronal (Y={coronalSlice})</div>
    {/if}
    <SliceViewer
      {volumeMeta}
      plane="coronal"
      sliceIndex={coronalSlice}
      {layers}
      {crosshair}
      {showCrosshair}
      showSlider={showSliders}
      onCrosshairChange={handleCrosshairChange}
      onSliceChange={handleCoronalSliceChange}
      {onMouseWorldCoord}
      width={coronalWidth}
      height={coronalHeight}
    />
  </div>
  
  <div class="view-container">
    {#if showLabels}
      <div class="view-label">Sagittal (X={sagittalSlice})</div>
    {/if}
    <SliceViewer
      {volumeMeta}
      plane="sagittal"
      sliceIndex={sagittalSlice}
      {layers}
      {crosshair}
      {showCrosshair}
      showSlider={showSliders}
      onCrosshairChange={handleCrosshairChange}
      onSliceChange={handleSagittalSliceChange}
      {onMouseWorldCoord}
      width={sagittalWidth}
      height={sagittalHeight}
    />
  </div>
</div>

  .orthogonal-viewer {

  .orthogonal-horizontal {

  .orthogonal-grid .view-container:nth-child(1) {

  }

    position: relative;
    /* Ensure the container doesn't clip its children */
    overflow: visible;
    /* Make sure it fills the grid cell */
    width: 100%;
    height: 100%;
    display: flex;
    flex-direction: column;
  }
  
  .view-label {

    pointer-events: none;
