<file path="ui/src/lib/components/SliceViewer.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
  import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
  import { getGpuRenderer, initializeGpuRenderer } from '../gpu';
  import type { ViewFrameExplicit, VolumeMeta, Vec3, Plane } from '../geometry/types';
  import { 
    makeFrameExplicit, 
    pan as panFrame, 
    zoomAroundPoint, 
    advanceSlice,
    screenToWorld,
    getCurrentSliceIndex,
    createFrameVersionGenerator
  } from '../geometry/viewFrameExplicit';
  import type { LayerSpec } from '@brainflow/api';
  
  // Props
  export let volumeMeta: VolumeMeta;
  export let plane: Plane = 'axial';
  export let sliceIndex = 0;
  export let layers: LayerSpec[] = [];
  export let crosshair: Vec3 | null = null;
  export let showCrosshair = true;
  export let showSlider = true;
  export let onCrosshairChange: ((pos: Vec3) => void) | null = null;
  export let onSliceChange: ((index: number) => void) | null = null;
  export let onMouseWorldCoord: ((coords: [number, number, number] | null) => void) | null = null;
  export let width = 512;
  export let height = 512;
  
  // Internal state
  let canvas: HTMLCanvasElement;
  let ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D | null = null;
  let frame: ViewFrameExplicit;
  let animationFrameId: number | null = null;
  let isInteracting = false;
  let lastPointerPos = { x: 0, y: 0 };
  let renderPending = false;
  
  // Interaction state
  let isPanning = false;
  let isZooming = false;
  let wheelTimeout: number | null = null;
  
  // Computed max slice index
  $: maxSliceIndex = plane === 'axial' ? volumeMeta.dims.z - 1 :
                     plane === 'coronal' ? volumeMeta.dims.y - 1 :
                     volumeMeta.dims.x - 1;
  
  // Create version generator for this viewer instance
  const getNextVersion = createFrameVersionGenerator();
  
  // Initialize frame
  $: {
    const sliceMm = sliceIndex * (
      plane === 'axial' ? volumeMeta.spacing.z :
      plane === 'coronal' ? volumeMeta.spacing.y :
      volumeMeta.spacing.x
    );
    
    frame = makeFrameExplicit(
      volumeMeta,
      plane,
      sliceMm,
      1.0, // Initial zoom
      { x: 0, y: 0 }, // Initial pan
      { x: width, y: height },
      getNextVersion
    );
  }
  
  // Render loop
  async function render() {
    if (!ctx || renderPending || !canvas) return;
    
    try {
      renderPending = true;
      const renderer = getGpuRenderer();
      
      // Ensure render target matches canvas size
      await renderer.setRenderSize(canvas.width, canvas.height);
      
      const result = await renderer.render({
        frame,
        layers,
        crosshair,
        showCrosshair
      });
      
      // Verify dimensions match
      if (result.width !== canvas.width || result.height !== canvas.height) {
        console.error(`Dimension mismatch: canvas ${canvas.width}x${canvas.height}, result ${result.width}x${result.height}`);
        return;
      }
      
      // Create ImageData from result
      const imageData = new ImageData(
        new Uint8ClampedArray(result.imageData),
        result.width,
        result.height
      );
      
      // Draw to canvas
      ctx.putImageData(imageData, 0, 0);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Render failed:', error);
    } finally {
      renderPending = false;
    }
  }
  
  // Animation frame loop for smooth interactions
  function startAnimationLoop() {
    if (animationFrameId !== null) return;
    
    function loop() {
      if (isInteracting && !renderPending) {
        render();
      }
      
      // Continue loop only if still interacting
      if (isInteracting) {
        animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
      } else {
        animationFrameId = null;
      }
    }
    
    animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  
  function stopAnimationLoop() {
    if (animationFrameId !== null) {
      cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId);
      animationFrameId = null;
    }
  }
  
  // Pointer event handlers
  function handlePointerDown(e: PointerEvent) {
    canvas.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    lastPointerPos = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
    
    if (e.button === 0) { // Left button
      isPanning = true;
      isInteracting = true;
      startAnimationLoop();
    } else if (e.button === 2) { // Right button
      // Could be used for windowing in the future
      e.preventDefault();
    }
  }
  
  function handlePointerMove(e: PointerEvent) {
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const currentPos = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
    
    if (isPanning) {
      const dx = currentPos.x - lastPointerPos.x;
      const dy = currentPos.y - lastPointerPos.y;
      
      frame = panFrame(frame, dx, dy, getNextVersion);
      lastPointerPos = currentPos;
    }
    
    // Update mouse world coordinates for status bar
    if (onMouseWorldCoord) {
      const worldPos = screenToWorld(frame, currentPos);
      onMouseWorldCoord([worldPos.x, worldPos.y, worldPos.z]);
    }
  }
  
  function handlePointerUp(e: PointerEvent) {
    canvas.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    isPanning = false;
    isInteracting = false;
    
    // Final render to ensure high quality
    render();
  }
  
  function handlePointerLeave(e: PointerEvent) {
    // Clear mouse world coordinates when leaving canvas
    if (onMouseWorldCoord) {
      onMouseWorldCoord(null);
    }
  }
  
  function handleWheel(e: WheelEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const mousePos = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
    
    // Check if this is a zoom or slice scroll
    if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
      // Zoom
      const zoomFactor = e.deltaY > 0 ? 0.9 : 1.1;
      const worldPos = screenToWorld(frame, mousePos);
      frame = zoomAroundPoint(frame, worldPos, zoomFactor, getNextVersion);
      
      isZooming = true;
      isInteracting = true;
      startAnimationLoop();
    } else {
      // Slice scroll
      const delta = Math.sign(e.deltaY);
      const spacing = plane === 'axial' ? volumeMeta.spacing.z :
                      plane === 'coronal' ? volumeMeta.spacing.y :
                      volumeMeta.spacing.x;
      
      frame = advanceSlice(frame, delta, spacing, getNextVersion);
      
      // Update the external slice index
      const newIndex = getCurrentSliceIndex(frame, volumeMeta, plane);
      sliceIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(maxSliceIndex, Math.round(newIndex)));
      
      if (onSliceChange) {
        onSliceChange(sliceIndex);
      }
      
      isInteracting = true;
      startAnimationLoop();
    }
    
    // Clear previous timeout
    if (wheelTimeout !== null) {
      clearTimeout(wheelTimeout);
    }
    
    // Set timeout to stop interaction
    wheelTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      isZooming = false;
      isInteracting = false;
      render(); // Final high-quality render
    }, 150);
  }
  
  function handleDoubleClick(e: MouseEvent) {
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const clickPos = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
    
    // Set crosshair at click position
    if (onCrosshairChange) {
      const worldPos = screenToWorld(frame, clickPos);
      onCrosshairChange(worldPos);
    }
  }
  
  function handleSliderChange() {
    // Update frame to match slider position
    const spacing = plane === 'axial' ? volumeMeta.spacing.z :
                    plane === 'coronal' ? volumeMeta.spacing.y :
                    volumeMeta.spacing.x;
    
    const currentSliceIndex = getCurrentSliceIndex(frame, volumeMeta, plane);
    const sliceDelta = sliceIndex - Math.round(currentSliceIndex);
    
    if (sliceDelta !== 0) {
      frame = advanceSlice(frame, sliceDelta, spacing, getNextVersion);
      isInteracting = true;
      startAnimationLoop();
      
      // Stop interaction after a short delay
      setTimeout(() => {
        isInteracting = false;
        render();
      }, 50);
      
      if (onSliceChange) {
        onSliceChange(sliceIndex);
      }
    }
  }
  
  // Lifecycle
  onMount(async () => {
    // Initialize GPU renderer first
    try {
      await initializeGpuRenderer();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to initialize GPU renderer:', error);
      return;
    }
    
    ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', {
      willReadFrequently: false,
      desynchronized: true
    });
    
    if (!ctx) {
      console.error('Failed to get 2D context');
      return;
    }
    
    // Initial render
    render();
    
    // Prevent context menu on right click
    const contextMenuHandler = (e: Event) => e.preventDefault();
    canvas.addEventListener('contextmenu', contextMenuHandler);
    
    // Store handler for cleanup
    (canvas as any)._contextMenuHandler = contextMenuHandler;
  });
  
  onDestroy(() => {
    stopAnimationLoop();
    if (wheelTimeout !== null) {
      clearTimeout(wheelTimeout);
    }
    
    // Remove context menu handler
    if (canvas && (canvas as any)._contextMenuHandler) {
      canvas.removeEventListener('contextmenu', (canvas as any)._contextMenuHandler);
    }
  });
  
  // Track changes to props
  let prevLayers = layers;
  let prevCrosshair = crosshair;
  let prevShowCrosshair = showCrosshair;
  
  // React to prop changes
  $: if (ctx) {
    const layersChanged = prevLayers !== layers;
    const crosshairChanged = prevCrosshair !== crosshair;
    const showCrosshairChanged = prevShowCrosshair !== showCrosshair;
    
    if (layersChanged || crosshairChanged || showCrosshairChanged) {
      prevLayers = layers;
      prevCrosshair = crosshair;
      prevShowCrosshair = showCrosshair;
      render();
    }
  }
  
  // React to size changes
  $: if (ctx && (width || height)) {
    frame = makeFrameExplicit(
      volumeMeta,
      plane,
      getCurrentSliceIndex(frame, volumeMeta, plane) * (
        plane === 'axial' ? volumeMeta.spacing.z :
        plane === 'coronal' ? volumeMeta.spacing.y :
        volumeMeta.spacing.x
      ),
      frame.pixels_per_mm * Math.max(width / frame.viewport_px.x, height / frame.viewport_px.y),
      { x: 0, y: 0 }, // Reset pan on resize
      { x: width, y: height },
      getNextVersion
    );
    render();
  }
</script>

<div class="slice-viewer-container">
  <div class="slice-viewer">
    <canvas
      bind:this={canvas}
      {width}
      {height}
      on:pointerdown={handlePointerDown}
      on:pointermove={handlePointerMove}
      on:pointerup={handlePointerUp}
      on:pointercancel={handlePointerUp}
      on:pointerleave={handlePointerLeave}
      on:wheel={handleWheel}
      on:dblclick={handleDoubleClick}
    ></canvas>
  </div>
  
  {#if showSlider}
    <div class="slice-controls" style="width: {width}px;">
      <input
        type="range"
        class="slice-slider"
        min={0}
        max={maxSliceIndex}
        bind:value={sliceIndex}
        on:input={handleSliderChange}
      />
      <div class="slice-info">
        <span class="slice-label">{plane === 'axial' ? 'Z' : plane === 'coronal' ? 'Y' : 'X'}</span>
        <span class="slice-value">{sliceIndex} / {maxSliceIndex}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  {/if}
</div>

  .slice-viewer {
    /* Allow this element to grow and shrink to fill available space */
    flex: 1 1 auto;

    min-height: 0;
    position: relative;
    background: #000;

    touch-action: none;
  }
  
  canvas {
    /* Make the canvas responsive to its parent's size */

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/SliceViewer.test.ts">
import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/svelte';
import { tick } from 'svelte';
import SliceViewer from './SliceViewer.svelte';
import type { VolumeMeta } from '../geometry/types';
import { getGpuRenderer } from '../gpu';

// Polyfill ImageData for Node environment
if (typeof globalThis.ImageData === 'undefined') {
  (globalThis as any).ImageData = class ImageData {
    data: Uint8ClampedArray;
    width: number;
    height: number;
    
    constructor(data: Uint8ClampedArray, width: number, height: number) {
      this.data = data;
      this.width = width;
      this.height = height;
    }
  };
}

// Mock GPU renderer
vi.mock('../gpu', () => {
  const mockRender = vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({
    imageData: new Uint8Array(512 * 512 * 4),
    width: 512,
    height: 512,
    frameVersion: 1
  });
  const mockInitialize = vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined);
  
  return {
    getGpuRenderer: vi.fn(() => ({
      render: mockRender,
      initialize: mockInitialize
    })),
    initializeGpuRenderer: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({
      render: mockRender,
      initialize: mockInitialize
    })
  };
});

// Get mock functions after module is mocked
const { getGpuRenderer } = await import('../gpu');
const mockRender = (getGpuRenderer as any)().render;

describe('SliceViewer', () => {
  let volumeMeta: VolumeMeta;
  
  beforeEach(() => {
    // Clear mocks
    vi.clearAllMocks();
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    volumeMeta = {
      dims: { x: 256, y: 256, z: 128 },
      spacing: { x: 1.0, y: 1.0, z: 2.0 },
      origin: { x: -128, y: -128, z: -128 }
    };
    
    // Mock canvas context
    HTMLCanvasElement.prototype.getContext = vi.fn(() => ({
      putImageData: vi.fn(),
      clearRect: vi.fn()
    })) as any;
    
    // Mock pointer capture
    HTMLCanvasElement.prototype.setPointerCapture = vi.fn();
    HTMLCanvasElement.prototype.releasePointerCapture = vi.fn();
  });
  
  it('should render with default props', async () => {
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: { volumeMeta }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas');
    expect(canvas).toBeTruthy();
    expect(canvas?.width).toBe(512);
    expect(canvas?.height).toBe(512);
  });
  
  it('should render with custom size', async () => {
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: {
        volumeMeta,
        width: 256,
        height: 256
      }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas');
    expect(canvas?.width).toBe(256);
    expect(canvas?.height).toBe(256);
  });
  
  it('should handle pan interaction', async () => {
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: { volumeMeta }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas')!;
    
    // Clear render calls from initialization
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Start pan
    await fireEvent.pointerDown(canvas, {
      clientX: 100,
      clientY: 100,
      button: 0
    });
    
    // Move
    await fireEvent.pointerMove(canvas, {
      clientX: 150,
      clientY: 120
    });
    
    // The component uses requestAnimationFrame, so we need to wait
    await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
    
    // End pan
    await fireEvent.pointerUp(canvas);
    
    await tick();
    
    // Should have triggered renders during interaction
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
  
  it('should handle wheel zoom', async () => {
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: { volumeMeta }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas')!;
    
    // Clear render calls from initialization
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Zoom in
    await fireEvent.wheel(canvas, {
      deltaY: -100,
      ctrlKey: true
    });
    
    // Wait for animation frame
    await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
    
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
  
  it('should handle slice scrolling', async () => {
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: {
        volumeMeta,
        sliceIndex: 10, // Start at slice 10
        plane: 'axial'
      }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas')!;
    
    // Clear render calls from initialization
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Scroll down (previous slice)
    await fireEvent.wheel(canvas, {
      deltaY: 100,
      ctrlKey: false
    });
    
    // Wait for animation frame
    await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
    
    // Should have triggered a render
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
  
  it('should handle double-click for crosshair', async () => {
    let crosshairPos: any = null;
    
    const { container } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: {
        volumeMeta,
        onCrosshairChange: (pos) => {
          crosshairPos = pos;
        }
      }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    const canvas = container.querySelector('canvas')!;
    
    await fireEvent.dblClick(canvas, {
      clientX: 256,
      clientY: 256
    });
    
    expect(crosshairPos).toBeTruthy();
    expect(crosshairPos).toHaveProperty('x');
    expect(crosshairPos).toHaveProperty('y');
    expect(crosshairPos).toHaveProperty('z');
  });
  
  it('should update render when layers change', async () => {
    const { rerender } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: {
        volumeMeta,
        layers: []
      }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    // Clear render calls from initialization
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Update layers using rerender
    await rerender({
      volumeMeta,
      layers: [{
        volume_id: 'test-volume',
        opacity: 1.0,
        colormap_id: 0,
        window_level: 500,
        window_width: 1000
      }]
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
  
  it('should handle different planes', async () => {
    const { rerender } = render(SliceViewer, {
      props: {
        volumeMeta,
        plane: 'axial'
      }
    });
    
    await tick();
    
    // Clear render calls from initialization
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Change to coronal
    await rerender({
      volumeMeta,
      plane: 'coronal'
    });
    await tick();
    
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
    
    // Clear again
    mockRender.mockClear();
    
    // Change to sagittal
    await rerender({
      volumeMeta,
      plane: 'sagittal'
    });
    await tick();
    
    expect(mockRender).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
});

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/StatusBar.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	import { crosshairSlice } from '$lib/stores/crosshairSlice';
	import { useLayerStore } from '$lib/stores/layerStore';
	import { statusStore } from '$lib/stores/statusStore';
	import type { VolumeLayerGpuInfo, LayerSpec } from '@brainflow/api';
	import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
	
	// Subscribe to crosshair position
	const crosshair = $state({
		world: crosshairSlice.getState().crosshairWorldCoord
	});
	
	// Subscribe to crosshair changes
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = crosshairSlice.subscribe((state) => {
			crosshair.world = state.crosshairWorldCoord;
		});
		return unsubscribe;
	});
	
	// Mouse position state from status store
	let mouseWorldCoord = $state<[number, number, number] | null>(null);
	
	// Subscribe to status store for mouse coordinates
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = statusStore.subscribe((state) => {
			mouseWorldCoord = state.mouseWorldCoord;
		});
		return unsubscribe;
	});
	
	// Field of view state - will be calculated from layer info
	let fieldOfView = $state({
		anteriorPosterior: { min: -100, max: 100 },
		leftRight: { min: -100, max: 100 },
		inferiorSuperior: { min: -50, max: 50 }
	});
	
	// Layer intensity values at crosshair
	let layerIntensities = $state<Array<{ id: string; value: number | null }>>([]);
	
	// Helper function to get layer ID from spec
	function getLayerIdFromSpec(spec: LayerSpec): string | null {
		if (spec && 'Volume' in spec) {
			return spec.Volume.id;
		}
		return null;
	}
	
	// Update FOV when layers change
	$effect(() => {
		const unsubscribe = useLayerStore.subscribe((state) => {
			// Get the first layer with GPU info
			const layerWithGpu = state.layers.find(l => l.gpu);
			if (layerWithGpu?.gpu && 'dim' in layerWithGpu.gpu) {
				updateFieldOfView(layerWithGpu.gpu as VolumeLayerGpuInfo);
			}
		});
		return unsubscribe;
	});
	
	
	// Sample intensities when crosshair changes
	$effect(() => {
		const coords = crosshair.world;
		if (!coords) {
			layerIntensities = [];
			return;
		}
		
		// Get all layers with volumes
		const layers = useLayerStore.getState().layers;
		
		// Sample each layer
		Promise.all(
			layers.map(async (layer) => {
				const layerId = getLayerIdFromSpec(layer.spec);
				if (!layerId || !layer.spec || !('Volume' in layer.spec)) {
					return null;
				}
				
				const volumeSpec = layer.spec.Volume;
				try {
					const value = await coreApi.sample_world_coordinate(
						volumeSpec.source_resource_id,
						coords
					);
					return { id: layerId, value };
				} catch (err) {
					console.error(`Failed to sample layer ${layerId}:`, err);
					return { id: layerId, value: null };
				}
			})
		).then(results => {
			layerIntensities = results.filter(r => r !== null) as Array<{ id: string; value: number | null }>;
		});
	});
	
	function updateFieldOfView(gpuInfo: VolumeLayerGpuInfo) {
		// Calculate world bounds from volume dimensions
		const dims = gpuInfo.dim;
		const origin = gpuInfo.origin;
		const spacing = gpuInfo.spacing;
		
		// For neuroimaging, typically:
		// X axis: Right (-) to Left (+) 
		// Y axis: Posterior (-) to Anterior (+)
		// Z axis: Inferior (-) to Superior (+)
		
		// Calculate bounds
		const xMin = Math.min(origin[0], origin[0] - (dims[0] - 1) * spacing[0]);
		const xMax = Math.max(origin[0], origin[0] - (dims[0] - 1) * spacing[0]);
		
		const yMin = Math.min(origin[1], origin[1] + (dims[1] - 1) * spacing[1]);
		const yMax = Math.max(origin[1], origin[1] + (dims[1] - 1) * spacing[1]);
		
		const zMin = Math.min(origin[2], origin[2] + (dims[2] - 1) * spacing[2]);
		const zMax = Math.max(origin[2], origin[2] + (dims[2] - 1) * spacing[2]);
		
		fieldOfView = {
			leftRight: { min: xMin, max: xMax },
			anteriorPosterior: { min: yMin, max: yMax },
			inferiorSuperior: { min: zMin, max: zMax }
		};
	}
	
	// Format coordinate for display
	function formatCoord(value: number): string {
		return value.toFixed(1);
	}
	
	// Format coordinate triple
	function formatCoordTriple(coords: [number, number, number] | null): string {
		if (!coords) return '—, —, —';
		return `${formatCoord(coords[0])}, ${formatCoord(coords[1])}, ${formatCoord(coords[2])}`;
	}
	
	// Format range
	function formatRange(min: number, max: number): string {
		return `[${formatCoord(min)}, ${formatCoord(max)}]`;
	}
</script>

<div class="status-bar">
	<div class="status-section">
		<span class="status-label">Crosshair:</span>
		<span class="status-value coordinate">{formatCoordTriple(crosshair.world)}</span>
	</div>
	
	<div class="status-divider"></div>
	
	<div class="status-section">
		<span class="status-label">Mouse:</span>
		<span class="status-value coordinate">{formatCoordTriple(mouseWorldCoord)}</span>
	</div>
	
	<div class="status-divider"></div>
	
	<div class="status-section fov-section">
		<span class="status-label">FOV:</span>
		<div class="fov-group">
			<span class="fov-item">
				<span class="fov-label">L/R:</span>
				<span class="fov-value">{formatRange(fieldOfView.leftRight.min, fieldOfView.leftRight.max)}</span>
			</span>
			<span class="fov-item">
				<span class="fov-label">A/P:</span>
				<span class="fov-value">{formatRange(fieldOfView.anteriorPosterior.min, fieldOfView.anteriorPosterior.max)}</span>
			</span>
			<span class="fov-item">
				<span class="fov-label">I/S:</span>
				<span class="fov-value">{formatRange(fieldOfView.inferiorSuperior.min, fieldOfView.inferiorSuperior.max)}</span>
			</span>
		</div>
	</div>
	
	<div class="status-divider"></div>
	
	<div class="status-section intensity-section">
		<span class="status-label">Intensity:</span>
		{#if layerIntensities.length === 0}
			<span class="status-value">—</span>
		{:else}
			<div class="intensity-group">
				{#each layerIntensities as layer}
					<span class="intensity-item">
						<span class="layer-id">{layer.id}:</span>
						<span class="intensity-value">{layer.value !== null ? layer.value.toFixed(1) : '—'}</span>
					</span>
				{/each}
			</div>
		{/if}
	</div>
</div>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/TreeBrowser.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	import { getContext, tick, onMount } from 'svelte';
	import type { ComponentContainer } from 'golden-layout';
    import { getGlContainer } from '$lib/layout/glUtils';
    import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
    import { useVolumeStore } from '$lib/stores/volumeStore'; // Corrected import
    import { useLayerStore } from '$lib/stores/layerStore'; // Import layer store
    import { nanoid } from 'nanoid'; // Import nanoid for layer IDs
    import type { LayerSpec, FlatNode, TreePayload } from '$lib/api'; // Import LayerSpec type (assuming it's exported from api.ts)
    // import { debug, error as logError } from 'tauri-plugin-log-api'; // 7. Added logger imports
    // import { icons } from '$lib/bridge_bindings'; // Assuming ts-rs generated icons here - COMMENTED OUT FOR NOW

    // --- Component State (Svelte 4 style) ---
    let container: ComponentContainer | undefined;
    let isLoading = false;
    let errorMsg: string | null = null;
    let rootDir = "/Users/bbuchsbaum/code/brainflow2/test-data"; // Default to test data directory
    let treeNodes: FlatNode[] = []; // State for the flat list of nodes
    let nodeMap = new Map<string, FlatNode>(); // Map ID to Node
    let childrenMap = new Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>(); // Map Parent ID to Children

    // --- Effects (Replaced with $: reactive blocks and onMount) ---
    onMount(async () => {
        // Fix: Call getGlContainer synchronously before any await
        container = getGlContainer();
        
        await tick();
        console.log("TreeBrowser initialized."); // Use console.log for now
        // Fetch initial directory listing
        loadDirectory(rootDir);
    });

    // Rebuild maps whenever treeNodes changes (Svelte 4 reactive statement)
    $: if (container) {
        console.log("Rebuilding tree maps triggered by treeNodes change..."); // Use console.log
        const newNodes = new Map<string, FlatNode>();
        const newChildren = new Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>();
        newChildren.set(null, []); // Initialize root children

        for (const [index, node] of treeNodes.entries()) {
            newNodes.set(node.id, node);
            const parentId = node.parent_idx !== null && node.parent_idx !== undefined && node.parent_idx < treeNodes.length 
                               ? treeNodes[node.parent_idx].id 
                               : null;

            if (!newChildren.has(parentId)) {
                newChildren.set(parentId, []);
            }
            newChildren.get(parentId)!.push(node); // Add node to parent's children list
        }
        // Sort children alphabetically (directories first, then files)
        for (const children of newChildren.values()) {
             children.sort((a, b) => {
                if (a.is_dir !== b.is_dir) {
                    return a.is_dir ? -1 : 1; // Directories first
                }
                return a.name.localeCompare(b.name); // Then alphabetical
             });
        }

        nodeMap = newNodes;
        childrenMap = newChildren;
        console.log("Tree maps rebuilt."); // Use console.log
    }

    // --- Event Handlers --- 
    
    // Generic handler for FileList or File[] input
    async function handleFiles(files: FileList | File[] | null) {
        if (!files || files.length === 0 || isLoading) return;
        
        isLoading = true;
        errorMsg = null;
        let successCount = 0;

        const fileArray = Array.from(files);

        for (const file of fileArray) {
            const nameParts = file.name.toLowerCase().split('.');
            let extension = '';
            if (nameParts.length > 1) {
                extension = nameParts.slice(-1)[0];
                if (extension === 'gz' && nameParts.length > 2) {
                    extension = nameParts.slice(-2).join('.');
                }
            }
            // debug(`Checking file: ${file.name}, detected ext: ${extension}`); // REMOVED log call
            console.log(`Checking file: ${file.name}, detected ext: ${extension}`);

            try {
                const filePathForApi = (file as any).path || file.name;
                // debug(`Calling coreApi.load_file for: ${filePathForApi}`); // REMOVED log call
                console.log(`Calling coreApi.load_file for: ${filePathForApi}`);
                const handleInfo = await coreApi.load_file(filePathForApi);
                // debug('File loaded successfully:', handleInfo); // REMOVED log call
                console.log('File loaded successfully:', handleInfo);
                
                useVolumeStore.getState().add(handleInfo);

                const layerId = `layer-${nanoid(5)}`;
                const defaultLayerSpec: LayerSpec = {
                    Volume: {
                        id: layerId,
                        source_resource_id: handleInfo.id,
                        colormap: 'grayscale',
                        slice_axis: null,
                        slice_index: null
                    }
                };
                // debug('Adding default layer spec:', defaultLayerSpec); // REMOVED log call
                console.log('Adding default layer spec:', defaultLayerSpec);
                useLayerStore.getState().addLayer(defaultLayerSpec);

                useLayerStore.getState().requestGpuResources(layerId);
                successCount++;

            } catch (error: unknown) {
                // debug(`Error loading file ${file.name}:`, error); // REMOVED log call
                console.error(`Error loading file ${file.name}:`, error);
                let message = `Failed to load ${file.name}.`;
                if (error instanceof Error) {
                    message = error.message;
                } else if (typeof error === 'string') {
                    message = error;
                } else if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'message' in error) {
                    message = String((error as any).message);
                }
                errorMsg = message; 
            }
        } 

        isLoading = false;
        if (successCount === 0 && fileArray.length > 0 && !errorMsg) {
            errorMsg = "No valid files found or loaded.";
        }
    }

    // --- Functions ---
    async function loadDirectory(dir: string) {
        if (isLoading) return;
        isLoading = true;
        errorMsg = null;
        treeNodes = []; // Clear previous nodes
        // debug(`Loading directory: ${dir}`); // REMOVED log call
        console.log(`Loading directory: ${dir}`);
        try {
            rootDir = dir; 
            const payload = await coreApi.fs_list_directory(dir);
            await tick(); 
            treeNodes = payload.nodes;
            // debug(`Loaded ${treeNodes.length} nodes.`); // REMOVED log call
            console.log(`Loaded ${treeNodes.length} nodes.`);
        } catch (error: any) {
            // logError(`Error listing directory ${dir}: ${JSON.stringify(error)}`); // REMOVED log call
            console.error(`Error listing directory ${dir}: ${JSON.stringify(error)}`);
            errorMsg = error?.message || 'Failed to list directory.';
            treeNodes = [];
        } finally {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    function handleNodeClick(node: FlatNode) {
        if (node.is_dir) {
            // debug(`Directory clicked: ${node.id}`); // REMOVED log call
            console.log(`Directory clicked: ${node.id}`);
            loadDirectory(node.id);
        } else {
            // debug(`File clicked: ${node.id}`); // REMOVED log call
            console.log(`File clicked: ${node.id}`);
            // Load single file using its full path (node.id contains the full path)
            handleSingleFile(node.id, node.name);
        }
    }

    async function handleSingleFile(fullPath: string, fileName: string) {
        if (isLoading) return;
        isLoading = true;
        errorMsg = null;

        try {
            // Check if it's a supported file type
            const nameParts = fileName.toLowerCase().split('.');
            let extension = '';
            if (nameParts.length > 1) {
                extension = nameParts.slice(-1)[0];
                if (extension === 'gz' && nameParts.length > 2) {
                    extension = nameParts.slice(-2).join('.');
                }
            }

            console.log(`Loading file: ${fileName} from path: ${fullPath}`);
            const handleInfo = await coreApi.load_file(fullPath);
            console.log('File loaded successfully:', handleInfo);
            
            useVolumeStore.getState().add(handleInfo);

            const layerId = `layer-${nanoid(5)}`;
            const defaultLayerSpec: LayerSpec = {
                Volume: {
                    id: layerId,
                    source_resource_id: handleInfo.id,
                    colormap: 'grayscale',
                    slice_axis: null,
                    slice_index: null
                }
            };
            console.log('Adding default layer spec:', defaultLayerSpec);
            useLayerStore.getState().addLayer(defaultLayerSpec);

            useLayerStore.getState().requestGpuResources(layerId);

        } catch (error: unknown) {
            console.error(`Error loading file ${fileName}:`, error);
            let message = `Failed to load ${fileName}.`;
            if (error instanceof Error) {
                message = error.message;
            } else if (typeof error === 'string') {
                message = error;
            } else if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'message' in error) {
                message = String((error as any).message);
            }
            errorMsg = message;
        } finally {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

</script>

<!-- Recursive Tree Node Component (Inline using svelte:self or separate file later) -->
{#snippet renderChildren(parentId: string | null)}
    {@const children = childrenMap.get(parentId)}
    {#if children && children.length > 0}
        <ul>
            {#each children as node (node.id)}
                {@const typedNode = node as FlatNode}
                <li onclick={() => handleNodeClick(typedNode)} title={typedNode.id}>
                    {#if typedNode.is_dir}
                        <span>&#128193; {typedNode.name}</span>
                        {@render renderChildren(typedNode.id)}
                    {:else}
                        <span>&#128196; {typedNode.name}</span>
                    {/if}
                </li>
            {/each}
        </ul>
    {/if}
{/snippet}

<div class="tree-browser-container">
    <div class="directory-controls">
        <input 
            type="text" 
            bind:value={rootDir} 
            placeholder="Enter directory path"
            class="directory-input"
        />
        <button onclick={() => loadDirectory(rootDir)} class="load-button">
            Load Directory
        </button>
    </div>
    <h4>File Browser: {rootDir}</h4>
    {#if isLoading}
        <div class="feedback loading">Loading {rootDir}...</div>
    {/if}
    {#if errorMsg}
        <div class="feedback error">Error: {errorMsg}</div>
    {/if}

    <!-- Basic Tree Placeholder -->
    <div class="tree-view">
        {#if isLoading}
            <!-- Optional: Add loading indicator inside tree-view too -->
            <p>Loading tree...</p> 
        {:else if errorMsg}
             <!-- Error message is already shown above, maybe just a note here -->
            <p>Failed to load directory tree.</p> 
        {:else if treeNodes.length > 0}
            <!-- Start rendering from the root (null parentId) -->
             {@render renderChildren(null)}
        {:else} <!-- Covers !isLoading && !errorMsg && treeNodes.length === 0 -->
            <p>Directory is empty or contains no loadable files.</p>
        {/if}
    </div>

    <!-- File Input Button -->
    <input 
        type="file" 
        multiple 
        accept=".nii,.nii.gz,.gii" 
        id="file-input" 
        style="display: none;" 
        onchange={(e) => handleFiles((e.target as HTMLInputElement).files)}
        disabled={isLoading}
        data-testid="tree-file-input" 
    />
    <button class="load-button" onclick={() => document.getElementById('file-input')?.click()} disabled={isLoading}>
        Browse Files...
    </button>

    <!-- Drag and Drop Zone -->
    <div 
        class="drop-zone" 
        class:loading={isLoading} 
        data-testid="tree-drop-zone"
        ondragover={(e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).classList.add('dragover');
        }}
        ondragleave={(e) => {
             e.preventDefault();
             (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).classList.remove('dragover');
        }}
        ondrop={(e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).classList.remove('dragover');
            handleFiles(e.dataTransfer?.files ?? null);
        }}
    >
        <p>...or drop NIfTI / GIfTI files here</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Placeholder for displaying loaded volumes/layers (can be separate component) -->
    <!-- <div class="loaded-items-list"> -->
        <!-- Placeholder -->
    <!-- </div> -->

</div>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/TreeBrowser.test.ts">
/**
 * TreeBrowser Component Tests
 * 
 * STATUS: Tests written but currently failing due to component initialization issues.
 * 
 * ISSUE: The TreeBrowser component calls loadDirectory() in onMount, which makes it
 * difficult to mock the API calls before they're made. The component needs refactoring
 * to be more testable.
 * 
 * TODO (Sprint 1): Refactor TreeBrowser to:
 * 1. Accept coreApi as an optional prop for dependency injection
 * 2. Move loadDirectory call to a method that can be controlled in tests
 * 3. Add loading state management that's more predictable
 * 
 * TICKET: Create follow-up ticket for "Refactor TreeBrowser for testability"
 * 
 * @see https://github.com/bbuchsbaum/brainflow2/issues/[TODO: CREATE ISSUE]
 */

import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
import { screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/svelte';
import TreeBrowser from './TreeBrowser.svelte';
import { renderComponent, waitForUpdates, mockTauriAPI } from '../../test/utils';
import type { TreePayload, FlatNode } from '$lib/api';

// Mock the API module to intercept calls
vi.mock('$lib/api', () => ({
  coreApi: {
    fs_list_directory: vi.fn(),
    load_file: vi.fn(),
  },
}));

// Import coreApi after mocking
import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';

// Mock the stores
vi.mock('$lib/stores/volumeStore', () => ({
  useVolumeStore: () => ({
    subscribe: vi.fn(),
    addVolume: vi.fn(),
  }),
}));

vi.mock('$lib/stores/layerStore', () => ({
  useLayerStore: () => ({
    subscribe: vi.fn(),
    addLayer: vi.fn(),
  }),
}));

// Mock the layout utilities
vi.mock('$lib/layout/glUtils', () => ({
  getGlContainer: vi.fn(() => ({
    setTitle: vi.fn(),
    on: vi.fn(),
  })),
}));

// Mock nanoid
vi.mock('nanoid', () => ({
  nanoid: () => 'test-id-123',
}));

describe('TreeBrowser', () => {
  let tauriMocks: ReturnType<typeof mockTauriAPI>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    vi.clearAllMocks();
    tauriMocks = mockTauriAPI();
  });

  it('renders loading state initially', async () => {
    // Mock fs_list_directory to return pending promise
    tauriMocks.mockInvoke.mockReturnValue(new Promise(() => {}));

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    
    expect(screen.getByText('Loading...')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('displays directory tree when loaded', async () => {
    const mockTreePayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [
        {
          id: '/root',
          name: 'root',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 0,
          is_dir: true,
        },
        {
          id: '/root/data',
          name: 'data',
          parent_idx: 0,
          icon_id: 0,
          is_dir: true,
        },
        {
          id: '/root/test.nii.gz',
          name: 'test.nii.gz',
          parent_idx: 0,
          icon_id: 2,
          is_dir: false,
        },
      ],
    };

    vi.mocked(coreApi.fs_list_directory).mockResolvedValue(mockTreePayload);

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    expect(screen.queryByText('Loading...')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByText('root')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByText('data')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByText('test.nii.gz')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('handles directory expansion', async () => {
    const initialPayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [
        {
          id: '/root',
          name: 'root',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 0,
          is_dir: true,
        },
        {
          id: '/root/data',
          name: 'data',
          parent_idx: 0,
          icon_id: 0,
          is_dir: true,
        },
      ],
    };

    const expandedPayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [
        ...initialPayload.nodes,
        {
          id: '/root/data/scan1.nii',
          name: 'scan1.nii',
          parent_idx: 1,
          icon_id: 2,
          is_dir: false,
        },
      ],
    };

    tauriMocks.mockInvoke
      .mockResolvedValueOnce(initialPayload)
      .mockResolvedValueOnce(expandedPayload);

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    // Click on data folder to expand
    const dataFolder = screen.getByText('data');
    await fireEvent.click(dataFolder);
    await waitForUpdates();

    expect(screen.getByText('scan1.nii')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('loads nifti file when clicked', async () => {
    const mockTreePayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [
        {
          id: '/root/brain.nii.gz',
          name: 'brain.nii.gz',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 2,
          is_dir: false,
        },
      ],
    };

    const mockVolumeId = 'volume-123';
    
    tauriMocks.mockInvoke
      .mockResolvedValueOnce(mockTreePayload) // fs_list_directory
      .mockResolvedValueOnce({ // load_file
        volume_id: mockVolumeId,
        metadata: {
          dims: [91, 109, 91],
          spacing: [2, 2, 2],
        },
      });

    const { container } = renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    // Click on the nifti file
    const niftiFile = screen.getByText('brain.nii.gz');
    await fireEvent.click(niftiFile);
    await waitForUpdates();

    // Verify load_file was called with correct path
    expect(tauriMocks.mockInvoke).toHaveBeenCalledWith('load_file', {
      path: '/root/brain.nii.gz',
    });
  });

  it('displays error when directory loading fails', async () => {
    const errorMessage = 'Permission denied';
    tauriMocks.mockInvoke.mockRejectedValue(new Error(errorMessage));

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    expect(screen.getByText(`Error: ${errorMessage}`)).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('handles empty directory', async () => {
    const emptyPayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [],
    };

    tauriMocks.mockInvoke.mockResolvedValue(emptyPayload);

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    expect(screen.getByText('(empty)')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('shows correct icons for different file types', async () => {
    const mockTreePayload: TreePayload = {
      nodes: [
        {
          id: '/folder',
          name: 'folder',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 0, // Folder icon
          is_dir: true,
        },
        {
          id: '/nifti.nii',
          name: 'nifti.nii',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 2, // NIfTI icon
          is_dir: false,
        },
        {
          id: '/gifti.gii',
          name: 'gifti.gii',
          parent_idx: null,
          icon_id: 3, // GIFTI icon
          is_dir: false,
        },
      ],
    };

    vi.mocked(coreApi.fs_list_directory).mockResolvedValue(mockTreePayload);

    renderComponent(TreeBrowser);
    await waitForUpdates();

    // Check that different icons are rendered (based on the icon class or aria-label)
    const folderIcon = screen.getByText('📁');
    const niftiIcon = screen.getByText('🧠');
    const giftiIcon = screen.getByText('🧠');

    expect(folderIcon).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(niftiIcon).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(giftiIcon).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});
</file>

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/TreeBrowserRefactored.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	/**
	 * @component TreeBrowserRefactored
	 * @description Refactored file browser with improved architecture and features
	 */
	import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
	import { coreApi as defaultCoreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import type { FlatNode, CoreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import { 
		Folder, 
		FolderOpen, 
		File, 
		FileType, 
		RefreshCw, 
		Home,
		ChevronRight,
		Search,
		X
	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	// Props
	let {
		rootDirectory = '.',
		coreApi = defaultCoreApi,
		acceptedExtensions = ['.nii', '.nii.gz', '.gii'],
		onFileSelected = (file: FlatNode) => {},
		onDirectoryChanged = (path: string) => {},
		onError = (error: Error) => {},
		showFileInfo = true,
		autoLoadOnMount = true
	}: {
		rootDirectory?: string;
		coreApi?: CoreApi;
		acceptedExtensions?: string[];
		onFileSelected?: (file: FlatNode) => void;
		onDirectoryChanged?: (path: string) => void;
		onError?: (error: Error) => void;
		showFileInfo?: boolean;
		autoLoadOnMount?: boolean;
	} = $props();

	// State
	let currentPath = $state(rootDirectory);
	let isLoading = $state(false);
	let searchQuery = $state('');
	let expandedDirs = $state(new Set<string>());
	let selectedNodeId = $state<string | null>(null);
	let treeNodes = $state<FlatNode[]>([]);
	let nodeMap = $state(new Map<string, FlatNode>());
	let childrenMap = $state(new Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>());
	let pathHistory = $state<string[]>([rootDirectory]);
	let historyIndex = $state(0);
	let error = $state<string | null>(null);

	// Directory cache for performance
	let directoryCache = new Map<string, { nodes: FlatNode[], timestamp: number }>();
	const CACHE_DURATION = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 minutes

	// Computed values
	let breadcrumbs = $derived(() => {
		const parts = currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
		if (currentPath === '/') return [{ name: '/', path: '/' }];
		
		return parts.map((part, index) => ({
			name: part,
			path: '/' + parts.slice(0, index + 1).join('/')
		}));
	});

	let filteredNodes = $derived(() => {
		if (!searchQuery) return treeNodes;
		
		const query = searchQuery.toLowerCase();
		return treeNodes.filter(node => 
			node.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)
		);
	});

	// Rebuild tree structure when nodes change
	$effect(() => {
		const newNodeMap = new Map<string, FlatNode>();
		const newChildrenMap = new Map<string | null, FlatNode[]>();
		newChildrenMap.set(null, []); // Root level

		for (const node of filteredNodes) {
			newNodeMap.set(node.id, node);
			
			const parentId = node.parent_idx !== null && node.parent_idx !== undefined && node.parent_idx < treeNodes.length
				? treeNodes[node.parent_idx].id
				: null;

			if (!newChildrenMap.has(parentId)) {
				newChildrenMap.set(parentId, []);
			}
			newChildrenMap.get(parentId)!.push(node);
		}

		// Sort children: directories first, then alphabetically
		for (const children of newChildrenMap.values()) {
			children.sort((a, b) => {
				if (a.is_dir !== b.is_dir) {
					return a.is_dir ? -1 : 1;
				}
				return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
			});
		}

		nodeMap = newNodeMap;
		childrenMap = newChildrenMap;
	});

	// Load directory contents
	async function loadDirectory(path: string, useCache = true) {
		if (isLoading) return;

		// Check cache first
		if (useCache) {
			const cached = directoryCache.get(path);
			if (cached && Date.now() - cached.timestamp < CACHE_DURATION) {
				treeNodes = cached.nodes;
				currentPath = path;
				onDirectoryChanged(path);
				return;
			}
		}

		isLoading = true;
		error = null;

		try {
			const payload = await coreApi.fs_list_directory(path);
			treeNodes = payload.nodes;
			
			// Update cache
			directoryCache.set(path, {
				nodes: payload.nodes,
				timestamp: Date.now()
			});

			currentPath = path;
			onDirectoryChanged(path);
			
			// Update history
			if (historyIndex < pathHistory.length - 1) {
				pathHistory = pathHistory.slice(0, historyIndex + 1);
			}
			pathHistory = [...pathHistory, path];
			historyIndex = pathHistory.length - 1;
			
		} catch (err) {
			console.error(`Error loading directory ${path}:`, err);
			error = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to load directory';
			onError(err instanceof Error ? err : new Error(String(err)));
			treeNodes = [];
		} finally {
			isLoading = false;
		}
	}

	// Handle node click
	function handleNodeClick(node: FlatNode) {
		if (node.is_dir) {
			if (expandedDirs.has(node.id)) {
				expandedDirs.delete(node.id);
			} else {
				expandedDirs.add(node.id);
			}
			loadDirectory(node.id);
		} else {
			selectedNodeId = node.id;
			
			// Check if file has accepted extension
			const hasValidExtension = acceptedExtensions.some(ext => 
				node.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext)
			);
			
			if (hasValidExtension) {
				onFileSelected(node);
			}
		}
	}

	// Navigation functions
	function navigateUp() {
		const parts = currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
		if (parts.length > 0) {
			parts.pop();
			const parentPath = parts.length > 0 ? '/' + parts.join('/') : '/';
			loadDirectory(parentPath);
		}
	}

	function navigateBack() {
		if (historyIndex > 0) {
			historyIndex--;
			loadDirectory(pathHistory[historyIndex], false);
		}
	}

	function navigateForward() {
		if (historyIndex < pathHistory.length - 1) {
			historyIndex++;
			loadDirectory(pathHistory[historyIndex], false);
		}
	}

	function navigateHome() {
		loadDirectory(rootDirectory);
	}

	function refresh() {
		loadDirectory(currentPath, false);
	}

	// Get file icon based on extension
	function getFileIcon(filename: string) {
		const ext = filename.toLowerCase();
		if (ext.endsWith('.nii') || ext.endsWith('.nii.gz')) {
			return '🧠'; // Brain icon for NIfTI
		} else if (ext.endsWith('.gii')) {
			return '🔺'; // Triangle for surface files
		}
		return '📄';
	}

	// Format file size
	function formatFileSize(bytes?: number): string {
		if (!bytes) return '';
		const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
		let size = bytes;
		let unitIndex = 0;
		
		while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
			size /= 1024;
			unitIndex++;
		}
		
		return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
	}

	// Clear search
	function clearSearch() {
		searchQuery = '';
	}

	// Lifecycle
	onMount(() => {
		if (autoLoadOnMount) {
			loadDirectory(currentPath);
		}
	});

	onDestroy(() => {
		// Clear cache on destroy
		directoryCache.clear();
	});

	// Recursive tree rendering
	function TreeNode(props: { node: FlatNode; depth: number }) {
		const { node, depth } = props;
		const children = childrenMap.get(node.id) || [];
		const isExpanded = expandedDirs.has(node.id);
		const isSelected = selectedNodeId === node.id;
		const hasValidExtension = !node.is_dir && acceptedExtensions.some(ext => 
			node.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext)
		);

		return {
			// Return render function
			render: () => (
				<>
					<div 
						class="tree-node"
						class:selected={isSelected}
						class:valid-file={hasValidExtension}
						style={`padding-left: ${depth * 20}px`}
						onclick={() => handleNodeClick(node)}
						role="button"
						tabindex="0"
					>
						<span class="node-icon">
							{#if node.is_dir}
								{#if isExpanded}
									<FolderOpen size={16} />
								{:else}
									<Folder size={16} />
								{/if}
							{:else}
								{#if hasValidExtension}
									<FileType size={16} />
								{:else}
									<File size={16} />
								{/if}
							{/if}
						</span>
						<span class="node-name">{node.name}</span>
						{#if showFileInfo && !node.is_dir && node.size}
							<span class="node-size">{formatFileSize(node.size)}</span>
						{/if}
					</div>
					{#if node.is_dir && isExpanded}
						{#each children as child}
							<TreeNode node={child} depth={depth + 1} />
						{/each}
					{/if}
				</>
			)
		};
	}
</script>

<div class="tree-browser-refactored">
	<!-- Header with navigation -->
	<div class="tree-header">
		<div class="nav-buttons">
			<button 
				onclick={navigateBack} 
				disabled={historyIndex === 0}
				title="Back"
				class="icon-button"
			>
				<ChevronRight size={16} style="transform: rotate(180deg)" />
			</button>
			<button 
				onclick={navigateForward} 
				disabled={historyIndex === pathHistory.length - 1}
				title="Forward"
				class="icon-button"
			>
				<ChevronRight size={16} />
			</button>
			<button 
				onclick={navigateUp}
				title="Up"
				class="icon-button"
			>
				<ChevronRight size={16} style="transform: rotate(-90deg)" />
			</button>
			<button 
				onclick={navigateHome}
				title="Home"
				class="icon-button"
			>
				<Home size={16} />
			</button>
			<button 
				onclick={refresh}
				disabled={isLoading}
				title="Refresh"
				class="icon-button"
			>
				<RefreshCw size={16} class:spinning={isLoading} />
			</button>
		</div>
		
		<!-- Search -->
		<div class="search-box">
			<Search size={16} />
			<input 
				type="text"
				placeholder="Search files..."
				bind:value={searchQuery}
				class="search-input"
			/>
			{#if searchQuery}
				<button onclick={clearSearch} class="clear-search">
					<X size={16} />
				</button>
			{/if}
		</div>
	</div>

	<!-- Breadcrumb navigation -->
	<div class="breadcrumbs">
		{#each breadcrumbs() as crumb, i}
			{#if i > 0}
				<span class="separator">/</span>
			{/if}
			<button 
				class="breadcrumb"
				onclick={() => loadDirectory(crumb.path)}
			>
				{crumb.name}
			</button>
		{/each}
	</div>

	<!-- Error display -->
	{#if error}
		<div class="error-message">
			{error}
		</div>
	{/if}

	<!-- Tree view -->
	<div class="tree-view">
		{#if isLoading}
			<div class="loading-state">
				<RefreshCw size={20} class="spinning" />
				<span>Loading directory...</span>
			</div>
		{:else if filteredNodes.length === 0}
			<div class="empty-state">
				{#if searchQuery}
					<p>No files match "{searchQuery}"</p>
				{:else}
					<p>Directory is empty</p>
				{/if}
			</div>
		{:else}
			{#each childrenMap.get(null) || [] as rootNode}
				<TreeNode node={rootNode} depth={0} />
			{/each}
		{/if}
	</div>
</div>

<style>
	.tree-browser-refactored {
		display: flex;
		flex-direction: column;
		height: 100%;
		background-color: var(--bg-primary, #1a1a1a);
		color: var(--text-primary, #e0e0e0);
		font-size: 14px;
	}

	.tree-header {
		display: flex;
		align-items: center;
		gap: 10px;
		padding: 10px;
		border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border-color, #333);
		background-color: var(--bg-secondary, #242424);

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/TreeBrowserRefactored.test.ts">
import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach, afterEach } from 'vitest';
import { render, fireEvent, waitFor } from '@testing-library/svelte';
import TreeBrowserRefactored from './TreeBrowserRefactored.svelte';
import type { FlatNode, TreePayload, CoreApi } from '$lib/api';

// Mock data
const mockNodes: FlatNode[] = [
  { id: '/home', name: 'home', is_dir: true, parent_idx: null },
  { id: '/home/user', name: 'user', is_dir: true, parent_idx: 0 },
  { id: '/home/user/data', name: 'data', is_dir: true, parent_idx: 1 },
  { id: '/home/user/data/brain.nii.gz', name: 'brain.nii.gz', is_dir: false, parent_idx: 2, size: 1024000 },
  { id: '/home/user/data/mask.nii', name: 'mask.nii', is_dir: false, parent_idx: 2, size: 512000 },
  { id: '/home/user/data/surface.gii', name: 'surface.gii', is_dir: false, parent_idx: 2, size: 2048000 },
  { id: '/home/user/data/readme.txt', name: 'readme.txt', is_dir: false, parent_idx: 2, size: 1024 },
];

const mockTreePayload: TreePayload = {
  nodes: mockNodes
};

// Mock CoreApi
const createMockCoreApi = () => ({
  fs_list_directory: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(mockTreePayload),
  load_file: vi.fn(),
  // Add other methods as needed
} as unknown as CoreApi);

describe('TreeBrowserRefactored', () => {
  let mockCoreApi: CoreApi;
  let mockOnFileSelected: ReturnType<typeof vi.fn>;
  let mockOnDirectoryChanged: ReturnType<typeof vi.fn>;
  let mockOnError: ReturnType<typeof vi.fn>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockCoreApi = createMockCoreApi();
    mockOnFileSelected = vi.fn();
    mockOnDirectoryChanged = vi.fn();
    mockOnError = vi.fn();
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    vi.clearAllMocks();
  });

  it('should render without loading on mount when autoLoadOnMount is false', async () => {
    const { container } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        autoLoadOnMount: false,
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    // Should not call fs_list_directory on mount
    expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    
    // Should show initial UI elements
    expect(container.querySelector('.tree-browser-refactored')).toBeTruthy();
    expect(container.querySelector('.tree-header')).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('should load directory on mount when autoLoadOnMount is true', async () => {
    render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home',
        autoLoadOnMount: true,
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).toHaveBeenCalledWith('/home');
    });
  });

  it('should display files and directories correctly', async () => {
    const { container, getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home',
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(getByText('home')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    // Click on home directory to expand
    fireEvent.click(getByText('home'));

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).toHaveBeenCalledWith('/home');
    });
  });

  it('should filter files by accepted extensions', async () => {
    const { container, getByText, queryByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        acceptedExtensions: ['.nii', '.nii.gz', '.gii'],
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      // Valid files should be visible
      expect(getByText('brain.nii.gz')).toBeTruthy();
      expect(getByText('mask.nii')).toBeTruthy();
      expect(getByText('surface.gii')).toBeTruthy();
      
      // Non-accepted file should still be visible but styled differently
      expect(getByText('readme.txt')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    // Valid files should have the valid-file class
    const brainNode = getByText('brain.nii.gz').closest('.tree-node');
    expect(brainNode?.classList.contains('valid-file')).toBe(true);

    // Invalid file should not have the class
    const readmeNode = getByText('readme.txt').closest('.tree-node');
    expect(readmeNode?.classList.contains('valid-file')).toBe(false);
  });

  it('should call onFileSelected when clicking on valid file', async () => {
    const { getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        acceptedExtensions: ['.nii', '.nii.gz', '.gii'],
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(getByText('brain.nii.gz')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    fireEvent.click(getByText('brain.nii.gz'));

    expect(mockOnFileSelected).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
      expect.objectContaining({
        id: '/home/user/data/brain.nii.gz',
        name: 'brain.nii.gz',
        is_dir: false
      })
    );
  });

  it('should not call onFileSelected for non-accepted files', async () => {
    const { getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        acceptedExtensions: ['.nii', '.nii.gz', '.gii'],
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(getByText('readme.txt')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    fireEvent.click(getByText('readme.txt'));

    expect(mockOnFileSelected).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('should handle search functionality', async () => {
    const { container, getByPlaceholderText, getByText, queryByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(getByText('brain.nii.gz')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    const searchInput = getByPlaceholderText('Search files...');
    
    // Search for "brain"
    await fireEvent.input(searchInput, { target: { value: 'brain' } });

    // Should show matching file
    expect(getByText('brain.nii.gz')).toBeTruthy();
    
    // Should hide non-matching files
    expect(queryByText('mask.nii')).toBeFalsy();
    expect(queryByText('surface.gii')).toBeFalsy();
  });

  it('should handle navigation buttons', async () => {
    const { container } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home',
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).toHaveBeenCalledWith('/home');
    });

    // Navigate to a subdirectory
    (mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory as any).mockResolvedValueOnce({ nodes: [] });
    
    const refreshButton = container.querySelector('[title="Refresh"]');
    expect(refreshButton).toBeTruthy();
    
    fireEvent.click(refreshButton!);

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(2);
    });
  });

  it('should handle errors gracefully', async () => {
    const errorMessage = 'Permission denied';
    (mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory as any).mockRejectedValueOnce(new Error(errorMessage));

    const { container, getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/restricted',
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(getByText(errorMessage)).toBeTruthy();
      expect(mockOnError).toHaveBeenCalledWith(expect.any(Error));
    });
  });

  it('should display file sizes correctly', async () => {
    const { getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        showFileInfo: true,
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      // Should format file sizes
      expect(getByText('1.0 MB')).toBeTruthy(); // brain.nii.gz
      expect(getByText('500.0 KB')).toBeTruthy(); // mask.nii
      expect(getByText('2.0 MB')).toBeTruthy(); // surface.gii
      expect(getByText('1.0 KB')).toBeTruthy(); // readme.txt
    });
  });

  it('should handle breadcrumb navigation', async () => {
    const { container, getByText } = render(TreeBrowserRefactored, {
      props: {
        coreApi: mockCoreApi,
        rootDirectory: '/home/user/data',
        onFileSelected: mockOnFileSelected,
        onDirectoryChanged: mockOnDirectoryChanged,
        onError: mockOnError
      }
    });

    await waitFor(() => {
      // Should show breadcrumbs
      expect(getByText('home')).toBeTruthy();
      expect(getByText('user')).toBeTruthy();
      expect(getByText('data')).toBeTruthy();
    });

    // Click on 'user' breadcrumb
    const userBreadcrumb = container.querySelectorAll('.breadcrumb')[1]; // Second breadcrumb
    fireEvent.click(userBreadcrumb);

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(mockCoreApi.fs_list_directory).toHaveBeenCalledWith('/home/user');
    });
  });
});

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/ViewerWithStatusBar.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
  import StatusBar from './StatusBar.svelte';
  import SliceViewer from './SliceViewer.svelte';
  import OrthogonalViewer from './OrthogonalViewer.svelte';
  import type { VolumeMeta, Vec3, Plane } from '../geometry/types';
  import type { LayerSpec } from '@brainflow/api';
  import { crosshairSlice } from '../stores/crosshairSlice';
  
  // Props
  export let volumeMeta: VolumeMeta;
  export let layers: LayerSpec[] = [];
  export let viewMode: 'single' | 'orthogonal' = 'single';
  export let plane: Plane = 'axial';
  export let width = 512;
  export let height = 512;
  
  let statusBar: StatusBar;
  
  // Handle mouse world coordinate updates
  function handleMouseWorldCoord(coords: [number, number, number] | null) {
    if (statusBar) {
      statusBar.setMouseWorldCoord(coords);
    }
  }
  
  // Handle crosshair changes
  function handleCrosshairChange(pos: Vec3) {
    // Update the global crosshair store
    crosshairSlice.getState().setCrosshairWorldCoord([pos.x, pos.y, pos.z]);
  }
</script>

<div class="viewer-with-status">
  <div class="viewer-container">
    {#if viewMode === 'single'}
      <SliceViewer
        {volumeMeta}
        {layers}
        {plane}
        {width}
        {height}
        showSlider={true}
        showCrosshair={true}
        onCrosshairChange={handleCrosshairChange}
        onMouseWorldCoord={handleMouseWorldCoord}
      />
    {:else}
      <OrthogonalViewer
        {volumeMeta}
        {layers}
        viewSize={Math.min(width, height) / 2}
        showCrosshair={true}
        showSliders={true}
        showLabels={true}
        onMouseWorldCoord={handleMouseWorldCoord}
      />
    {/if}
  </div>
  
  <StatusBar bind:this={statusBar} />
</div>

<style>
  .viewer-with-status {
    display: flex;
    flex-direction: column;
    height: 100%;
  }
  
  .viewer-container {
    flex: 1;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    background: #1a1a1a;
    overflow: auto;
  }
</style>
